// ==================== SRC/INDEX.JS ====================
const server = require('./server');
const config = require('./config');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');

async function startServer() {
  try {
    // Inicializar conexões
    await require('./config/database').connect();
    await require('./config/redis').connect();
    
    // Iniciar workers em modo produção
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
      require('./queues/workers/task.worker');
      require('./queues/workers/ai.worker');
    }
    
    const app = require('./app');
    const port = config.port || 3000;
    
    server.start(app, port);
    
    // Graceful shutdown
    process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
      logger.info('SIGTERM received, shutting down gracefully');
      server.stop();
    });
    
    process.on('SIGINT', () => {
      logger.info('SIGINT received, shutting down gracefully');
      server.stop();
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

startServer();

// ==================== SRC/SERVER.JS ====================
const http = require('http');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');

let serverInstance = null;

module.exports = {
  start: (app, port) => {
    serverInstance = http.createServer(app);
    
    serverInstance.listen(port, () => {
      logger.info(`Server running on port ${port}`);
      logger.info(`REST API: http://localhost:${port}/api`);
      logger.info(`GraphQL: http://localhost:${port}/graphql`);
      logger.info(`Dashboard: http://localhost:${port}`);
      logger.info(`Health: http://localhost:${port}/api/health`);
    });
    
    serverInstance.on('error', (error) => {
      if (error.code === 'EADDRINUSE') {
        logger.error(`Port ${port} is already in use`);
        process.exit(1);
      } else {
        logger.error('Server error:', error);
      }
    });
  },
  
  stop: async () => {
    if (serverInstance) {
      logger.info('Closing server...');
      
      // Fechar conexões
      const database = require('./config/database');
      const redis = require('./config/redis');
      const queues = require('./queues');
      
      await queues.closeAll();
      await redis.disconnect();
      await database.disconnect();
      
      serverInstance.close(() => {
        logger.info('Server closed');
        process.exit(0);
      });
      
      // Force shutdown after 10s
      setTimeout(() => {
        logger.error('Could not close connections in time, forcefully shutting down');
        process.exit(1);
      }, 10000);
    }
  }
};

// ==================== SRC/APP.JS ====================
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const compression = require('compression');
const winston = require('winston');
const expressWinston = require('express-winston');
const promBundle = require('express-prom-bundle');

const config = require('./config');
const apiRouter = require('./api');
const errorHandler = require('./middleware/errorHandler');
const rateLimit = require('./middleware/rateLimit');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');

const app = express();

// Metrics middleware
const metricsMiddleware = promBundle({
  includeMethod: true,
  includePath: true,
  includeStatusCode: true,
  includeUp: true,
  customLabels: { project: 'diyapp_v10' },
  promClient: { collectDefaultMetrics: {} }
});

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"]
    }
  }
}));

// CORS configuration
app.use(cors({
  origin: config.corsOrigins || ['http://localhost:3000'],
  credentials: true,
  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
  allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Request-ID']
}));

// Compression
app.use(compression());

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Request logging
app.use(expressWinston.logger({
  winstonInstance: logger,
  meta: true,
  msg: 'HTTP {{req.method}} {{req.url}} {{res.statusCode}} {{res.responseTime}}ms',
  expressFormat: true,
  colorize: false,
  ignoreRoute: (req) => req.path === '/api/health'
}));

// Metrics
app.use(metricsMiddleware);

// Rate limiting
app.use('/api/', rateLimit.api);
app.use('/graphql', rateLimit.graphql);

// Static files (Dashboard)
app.use(express.static('public'));

// API Routes
app.use('/api', apiRouter);

// GraphQL endpoint
if (config.graphqlEnabled) {
  const graphqlRouter = require('./api/graphql');
  app.use('/graphql', graphqlRouter);
}

// API Documentation
if (config.swaggerEnabled) {
  const swaggerUi = require('swagger-ui-express');
  const YAML = require('yaml');
  const fs = require('fs');
  const swaggerDocument = YAML.parse(fs.readFileSync('./docs/api-spec.yaml', 'utf8'));
  app.use('/api-docs', swaggerUi.serve, swaggerUi.setup(swaggerDocument));
}

// 404 handler
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Route ${req.method} ${req.path} not found`,
    request_id: req.headers['x-request-id'] || req.id
  });
});

// Error handling (must be last)
app.use(errorHandler);

module.exports = app;

// ==================== SRC/CONFIG/INDEX.JS ====================
require('dotenv').config();

module.exports = {
  // Server
  port: process.env.PORT || 3000,
  nodeEnv: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  
  // API
  apiVersion: process.env.API_VERSION || 'v1',
  graphqlEnabled: process.env.GRAPHQL_ENABLED === 'true',
  swaggerEnabled: process.env.SWAGGER_ENABLED !== 'false',
  
  // Security
  jwtSecret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'diyapp-v10-secret-change-in-production',
  jwtExpiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
  corsOrigins: process.env.CORS_ORIGINS ? process.env.CORS_ORIGINS.split(',') : ['http://localhost:3000'],
  
  // Rate limiting
  rateLimitWindow: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS) || 15 * 60 * 1000,
  rateLimitMax: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX) || 100,

  anthropicApiKey: process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY,
  defaultAiProvider: process.env.DEFAULT_AI_PROVIDER || 'openai',
  aiTimeout: parseInt(process.env.AI_TIMEOUT_MS) || 30000,
  aiMaxTokens: parseInt(process.env.AI_MAX_TOKENS) || 4000,

  // Database
  databaseUrl: process.env.DATABASE_URL || 'postgresql://postgres:password@localhost:5432/diyapp',
  databaseLogging: process.env.DATABASE_LOGGING === 'true',
  
  // Monitoring
  logLevel: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  metricsEnabled: process.env.METRICS_ENABLED !== 'false'

// ==================== SRC/CONFIG/DATABASE.JS ====================
const { Sequelize } = require('sequelize');
const config = require('./index');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

let sequelize = null;

module.exports = {
  connect: async () => {
    try {
      sequelize = new Sequelize(config.databaseUrl, {
        logging: config.databaseLogging ? (msg) => logger.debug(msg) : false,
        pool: {
          max: 10,
          min: 0,
          acquire: 30000,
          idle: 10000
        },
        retry: {
          max: 3,
          timeout: 10000,
          match: [
            /ConnectionError/,
            /SequelizeConnectionError/,
            /ECONNREFUSED/,
            /ETIMEDOUT/
          ]
        }
      });
      
      await sequelize.authenticate();
      logger.info('Database connection established successfully');
      
      // Sync models (em desenvolvimento)
      if (config.nodeEnv === 'development') {
        await sequelize.sync({ alter: true });
        logger.info('Database synced');
      }
      
      return sequelize;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Unable to connect to database:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  },
  
  getInstance: () => {
    if (!sequelize) {
      throw new Error('Database not initialized. Call connect() first.');
    }
    return sequelize;
  },
  
  disconnect: async () => {
    if (sequelize) {
      await sequelize.close();
      logger.info('Database connection closed');
    }
  }
};

// ==================== SRC/CONFIG/REDIS.JS ====================
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const config = require('./index');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

let redisClient = null;
let subscriber = null;

module.exports = {
  connect: async () => {
    try {
      redisClient = new Redis(config.redisUrl, {
        maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
        retryStrategy: (times) => {
          const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
          return delay;
        },
        reconnectOnError: (err) => {
          const targetError = 'READONLY';
          if (err.message.includes(targetError)) {
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        }
      });
      
      subscriber = new Redis(config.redisUrl);
      
      redisClient.on('connect', () => {
        logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
      });
      
      redisClient.on('error', (error

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
Vou configurar um ambiente Docker completo com health checks, logging centralizado ELK e monitoramento Prometheus/Grafana. Aqui está a implementação profissional:

## 2. Arquivo Principal docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

x-logging: &default-logging
  driver: "json-file"
  options:
    max-size: "10m"
    max-file: "3"

x-healthcheck: &default-healthcheck
  interval: 30s
  timeout: 10s
  retries: 3
  start_period: 40s

services:
  # API Service
  api:
    build: ./services/api
    container_name: diyapp-api
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://postgres:password@db:5432/diyapp
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
      - METRICS_PORT=9091
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:3000/health"]
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
      - monitoring-network
    depends_on:
      db:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    labels:
      - "prometheus.enable=true"
      - "prometheus.port=9091"
      - "prometheus.path=/metrics"

  # Frontend Service
  frontend:
    build: ./services/frontend
    container_name: diyapp-frontend
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:80/health"]
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
      - monitoring-network

  # Worker Service
  worker:
    build: ./services/worker
    container_name: diyapp-worker
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://postgres:password@db:5432/diyapp
      - LOG_LEVEL=info
    healthcheck:
      <<: *default-healthcheck
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pgrep -f 'node worker.js' || exit 1"]
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
      - monitoring-network
    depends_on:
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      db:
        condition: service_healthy

  # Database (PostgreSQL)
  db:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-db
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=diyapp
      - POSTGRES_USER=postgres
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=password
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init-db.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U postgres"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"

  # Redis
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    restart: unless-stopped
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    logging: *default-logging
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"

  # Prometheus
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ./docker/prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - ./docker/prometheus/alerts:/etc/prometheus/alerts
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:9090/-/healthy"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    networks:
      - monitoring-network
    labels:
      - "logging=prometheus"

  # Grafana
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin
      - GF_USERS_ALLOW_SIGN_UP=false
      - GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS=grafana-piechart-panel
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./docker/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
      - ./docker/grafana/dashboards:/etc/grafana/dashboards
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:3000/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    networks:
      - monitoring-network
    depends_on:
      prometheus:
        condition: service_healthy

  # Elasticsearch
  elasticsearch:
    image: docker.elastic.co/elasticsearch/elasticsearch:8.11.0
    container_name: diyapp-elasticsearch
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - discovery.type=single-node
      - xpack.security.enabled=false
      - "ES_JAVA_OPTS=-Xms512m -Xmx512m"
      - cluster.name=diyapp-cluster
    volumes:
      - elasticsearch_data:/usr/share/elasticsearch/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "curl -s http://localhost:9200/_cluster/health | grep -q '\"status\":\"green\"'"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5
    ports:
      - "9200:9200"
      - "9300:9300"
    networks:
      - logging-network
    ulimits:
      memlock:
        soft: -1
        hard: -1

  # Logstash
  logstash:
    image: docker.elastic.co/logstash/logstash:8.11.0
    container_name: diyapp-logstash
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ./docker/logstash/logstash.conf:/usr/share/logstash/pipeline/logstash.conf
      - ./docker/logstash/patterns:/usr/share/logstash/patterns
    environment:
      - LS_JAVA_OPTS=-Xmx256m -Xms256m
    ports:
      - "5000:5000"
      - "9600:9600"
    networks:
      - logging-network
      - monitoring-network
    depends_on:
      elasticsearch:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:9600/"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Kibana
  kibana:
    image: docker.elastic.co/kibana/kibana:8.11.0
    container_name: diyapp-kibana
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      - ELASTICSEARCH_HOSTS=http://elasticsearch:9200
    ports:
      - "5601:5601"
    networks:
      - logging-network
    depends_on:
      elasticsearch:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:5601/api/status"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Filebeat
  filebeat:
    image: docker.elastic.co/beats/filebeat:8.11.0
    container_name: diyapp-filebeat
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: root
    volumes:
      - ./docker/filebeat/filebeat.yml:/usr/share/filebeat/filebeat.yml
      - /var/lib/docker/containers:/var/lib/docker/containers:ro
      - /var/run/docker.sock:/var/run/docker.sock
    command: filebeat -e -strict.perms=false
    networks:
      - logging-network
    depends_on:
      logstash:
        condition: service_healthy

  # Node Exporter (System Metrics)
  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:latest
    container_name: diyapp-node-exporter
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /proc:/host/proc:ro
      - /sys:/host/sys:ro
      - /:/rootfs:ro
    command:
      - '--path.procfs=/host/proc'
      - '--path.rootfs=/rootfs'
      - '--path.sysfs=/host/sys'
      - '--collector.filesystem.mount-points-exclude=^/(sys|proc|dev|host|etc)($$|/)'
    ports:
      - "9100:9100"
    networks:
      - monitoring-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:9100/metrics"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # cAdvisor (Container Metrics)
  cadvisor:
    image: gcr.io/cadvisor/cadvisor:latest
    container_name: diyapp-cadvisor
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - /:/rootfs:ro
      - /var/run:/var/run:ro
      - /sys:/sys:ro
      - /var/lib/docker/:/var/lib/docker:ro
      - /dev/disk/:/dev/disk:ro
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    networks:
      - monitoring-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--no-verbose", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8080/healthz"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  # Alertmanager
  alertmanager:
    image: prom/alertmanager:latest
    container_name: diyapp-alertmanager
    restart: unless-stopped
    volumes:
      - ./docker/prometheus/alertmanager.yml:/etc/alertmanager/alertmanager.yml
      - alertmanager_data:/alertmanager
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/alertmanager/alertmanager.yml'
      - '--storage.path=/alertmanager'

      - "9093:9093"
    networks:
      - monitoring-network
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:9093/-/healthy"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
  monitoring-network:
    driver: bridge
  logging-network:
    driver: bridge

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:

  grafana_data:
  elasticsearch_data:
  alertmanager_data:

## 4. Dockerfiles dos Serviços

### services/api/Dockerfile
```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Install curl for health checks
RUN apk add --no-cache curl

# Copy package files
COPY package*.json ./

# Install dependencies
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source code
COPY src/ ./src/

# Create health check endpoint
RUN echo '#!/bin/sh\ncurl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1' > /usr/local/bin/healthcheck.sh \
    && chmod +x /usr/local/bin/healthcheck.sh

# Expose ports
EXPOSE 3000 9091

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=10s --start-period=40s --retries=3 \
    CMD curl -f http://localhost:3000/health || exit 1

# Start command
CMD ["node", "src/server.js"]
```

### services/api/src/health.js
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const redis = require('redis');

const dbPool = new Pool({
    connectionString: process.env.DATABASE_URL
});

const redisClient = redis.createClient({
    url: process.env.REDIS_URL
});

// Health check endpoint
router.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
    const health = {
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        checks: {
            api: 'healthy',
            database: 'unknown',
            redis: 'unknown',
            memory: 'healthy'
        }
    };

    try {
        // Check database
        const dbResult = await dbPool.query('SELECT 1 as healthy');
        health.checks.database = dbResult.rows[0].healthy === 1 ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy';
    } catch (error) {
        health.checks.database = 'unhealthy';
        health.status = 'degraded';
    }

    try {
        // Check Redis
        await redisClient.ping();
        health.checks.redis = 'healthy';
    } catch (error) {
        health.checks.redis = 'unhealthy';
        health.status = 'degraded';
    }

    // Check memory usage
    const used = process.memoryUsage();
    const memoryUsage = used.heapUsed / used.heapTotal;
    if (memoryUsage > 0.9) {
        health.checks.memory = 'warning';
        health.status = 'degraded';
    }

    const statusCode = health.status === 'healthy' ? 200 : 
                      health.status === 'degraded' ? 207 : 503;

    res.status(statusCode).json(health);
});

// Liveness probe
router.get('/health/liveness', (req, res) => {
    res.status(200).json({
        status: 'al

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - AI Ops Observabilidade

Vou implementar um sistema completo de observabilidade de IA em produção com foco em custo, qualidade, drift e governança de modelos. O sistema incluirá monitoramento de LLMs, cache Redis para otimização de custos, e sistema de fallback para modelos alternativos.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-ai-ops/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard principal
├── package.json
├── .env.example
├── README.md
├── src/
│   ├── server.js                 # Servidor principal
│   ├── config/
│   │   └── constants.js          # Configurações e constantes
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── aiOpsController.js    # Controlador AI Ops
│   │   ├── llmController.js      # Controlador LLM
│   │   └── metricsController.js  # Controlador de métricas
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── llmGateway.js         # Gateway para múltiplos provedores
│   │   ├── cacheService.js       # Serviço de cache Redis
│   │   ├── monitoringService.js  # Serviço de monitoramento
│   │   ├── qualityService.js     # Serviço de avaliação de qualidade
│   │   └── alertService.js       # Serviço de alertas
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── LLMCall.js            # Modelo de chamadas LLM
│   │   ├── CostMetric.js         # Modelo de métricas de custo
│   │   ├── QualityMetric.js      # Modelo de métricas de qualidade
│   │   └── Alert.js              # Modelo de alertas
│   ├── routes/
│   │   ├── aiOpsRoutes.js        # Rotas AI Ops
│   │   ├── llmRoutes.js          # Rotas LLM
│   │   └── metricsRoutes.js      # Rotas de métricas
│   ├── utils/
│   │   ├── logger.js             # Sistema de logging
│   │   ├── anomalyDetector.js    # Detector de anomalias
│   │   └── reportGenerator.js    # Gerador de relatórios
│   └── public/
│       ├── css/
│       │   └── styles.css        # Estilos do dashboard
│       ├── js/
│       │   └── dashboard.js      # JavaScript do dashboard
│       └── assets/
│           └── logos/            # Logos dos provedores
└── tests/
    ├── unit/
    └── integration/
```

## 3. src/server.js

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const compression = require('compression');
const dotenv = require('dotenv');
const path = require('path');
const socketIO = require('socket.io');
const http = require('http');

// Carregar variáveis de ambiente
dotenv.config();

// Importar configurações
const config = require('./config/constants');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');

// Importar rotas
const aiOpsRoutes = require('./routes/aiOpsRoutes');
const llmRoutes = require('./routes/llmRoutes');
const metricsRoutes = require('./routes/metricsRoutes');

// Inicializar app Express
const app = express();
const server = http.createServer(app);
const io = socketIO(server, {
    cors: {
        origin: "*",
        methods: ["GET", "POST"]
    }
});

// Middlewares
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
            defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
            styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net"],
            scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'", "https://cdn.jsdelivr.net", "https://cdn.socket.io"],
            connectSrc: ["'self'", "ws://localhost:3000", "wss://localhost:3000"]
        }
    }
}));
app.use(cors());
app.use(compression());
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// Servir arquivos estáticos
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// Rotas
app.use('/api/ai-ops', aiOpsRoutes);
app.use('/api/llm', llmRoutes);
app.use('/api/metrics', metricsRoutes);

// Rota principal - Dashboard
app.get('/', (req, res) => {
    res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

// Health Check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
    res.json({
        status: 'healthy',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        version: '1.0.0',
        services: {
            redis: 'connected',
            database: 'connected',
            monitoring: 'active'
        }
    });
});

// WebSocket para atualizações em tempo real
io.on('connection', (socket) => {
    logger.info('Novo cliente conectado via WebSocket');
    
    socket.on('subscribe', (channel) => {
        socket.join(channel);
        logger.info(`Cliente inscrito no canal: ${channel}`);
    });
    
    socket.on('disconnect', () => {
        logger.info('Cliente desconectado do WebSocket');
    });
});

// Injetar io nas requisições
app.use((req, res, next) => {
    req.io = io;
    next();
});

// Error handling middleware
app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
    logger.error('Erro não tratado:', err);
    res.status(500).json({
        error: 'Erro interno do servidor',
        message: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? err.message : undefined
    });
});

// Iniciar servidor
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;
server.listen(PORT, () => {
    logger.info(`🚀 Servidor AI Ops rodando na porta ${PORT}`);
    logger.info(`📊 Dashboard disponível em: http://localhost:${PORT}`);
    logger.info(`🔧 Modo: ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'}`);
});

module.exports = { app, server, io };
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
-- Database Schema v1.0
-- Data Engineer: Pipeline de Projetos e Execuções
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 1. SCHEMA PRINCIPAL
-- ============================================
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS diyapp_v10;
COMMENT ON SCHEMA diyapp_v10 IS 'Core database for DIYAPP Evolution V10 - Projects and Execution History';

-- ============================================
-- 2. TABELAS RAW (BRONZE LAYER)
-- ============================================

-- Tabela raw de projetos
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.raw_projects (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    project_config JSONB NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    created_by VARCHAR(100),
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'diyapp_api',
    raw_metadata JSONB,
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.raw_projects IS 'Raw project data from DIYAPP API';
COMMENT ON COLUMN diyapp_v10.raw_projects.project_config IS 'Complete project configuration JSON';
COMMENT ON COLUMN diyapp_v10.raw_projects.raw_metadata IS 'Additional metadata from source system';

-- Tabela raw de execuções
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.raw_executions (
    execution_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES diyapp_v10.raw_projects(project_id),
    execution_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    execution_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    start_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    resource_usage JSONB,
    error_details JSONB,
    output_metadata JSONB,
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'diyapp_executor',
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW(),
    raw_payload JSONB
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.raw_executions IS 'Raw execution logs from DIYAPP executor';
COMMENT ON COLUMN diyapp_v10.raw_executions.resource_usage IS 'CPU, memory, GPU usage metrics';
COMMENT ON COLUMN diyapp_v10.raw_executions.error_details IS 'Error stack trace and context';

-- Tabela raw de métricas de qualidade
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.raw_quality_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    execution_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES diyapp_v10.raw_executions(execution_id),
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value NUMERIC(15,6) NOT NULL,
    metric_threshold NUMERIC(15,6),
    metric_status VARCHAR(20),
    measured_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'diyapp_quality',
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.raw_quality_metrics IS 'Raw quality metrics from quality monitoring system';

-- ============================================
-- 3. TABELAS STAGING (SILVER LAYER)
-- ============================================

-- Staging de projetos (limpeza e padronização)
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.stg_projects (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    project_type VARCHAR(50),
    project_complexity VARCHAR(20),
    tech_stack JSONB,
    file_count INTEGER,
    total_lines_of_code INTEGER,
    has_frontend BOOLEAN,
    has_backend BOOLEAN,
    has_database BOOLEAN,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    created_by VARCHAR(100),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    staging_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.stg_projects IS 'Cleaned and standardized project data';

-- Staging de execuções
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.stg_executions (
    execution_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL,
    execution_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    execution_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    start_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    cpu_usage_percent NUMERIC(5,2),
    memory_usage_mb INTEGER,
    gpu_usage_percent NUMERIC(5,2),
    has_errors BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_severity VARCHAR(20),
    output_size_bytes INTEGER,
    staging_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.stg_executions IS 'Cleaned execution data with standardized metrics';

-- Staging de métricas de qualidade
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.stg_quality_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    execution_id UUID NOT NULL,
    metric_category VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    metric_value NUMERIC(15,6) NOT NULL,
    metric_threshold NUMERIC(15,6),
    metric_status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    is_critical BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    measured_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    staging_timestamp TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT NOW()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.stg_quality_metrics IS 'Standardized quality metrics with categorization';

-- ============================================
-- 4. TABELAS MARTS (GOLD LAYER)
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 4.1 MART DE PROJETOS (Product Manager)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_project_metrics (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL,
    project_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    project_type VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Métricas de atividade
    execution_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    successful_executions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    failed_executions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_execution_duration_ms NUMERIC(10,2),
    
    -- Métricas de qualidade
    avg_quality_score NUMERIC(5,2),
    critical_issues_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Métricas de uso
    total_cpu_seconds NUMERIC(15,2),
    total_memory_gb_hours NUMERIC(15,2),
    peak_memory_mb INTEGER,
    
    -- Métricas de crescimento
    first_execution_date DATE,
    last_execution_date DATE,
    days_active INTEGER,
    
    -- Agregações
    created_at DATE,
    project_age_days INTEGER,
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, project_id)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_project_metrics IS 'Daily project metrics for PM dashboards';

-- ============================================
-- 4.2 MART DE EXECUÇÕES (AI Ops)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_execution_analytics (
    hour TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    execution_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    project_type VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- Volume e performance
    execution_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    success_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    avg_duration_ms NUMERIC(10,2),
    p95_duration_ms NUMERIC(10,2),
    p99_duration_ms NUMERIC(10,2),
    
    -- Resource usage
    avg_cpu_percent NUMERIC(5,2),
    avg_memory_mb INTEGER,
    total_cpu_hours NUMERIC(15,4),
    
    -- Error analysis
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    most_common_error VARCHAR(100),
    error_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    
    -- Cost estimation (para LLM/GPU)
    estimated_cost_usd NUMERIC(10,4),
    
    PRIMARY KEY (hour, execution_type, project_type)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_execution_analytics IS 'Hourly execution analytics for AI Ops monitoring';

-- ============================================
-- 4.3 MART DE QUALIDADE (Especialista LLM)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_quality_trends (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    metric_category VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    metric_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Estatísticas
    sample_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    avg_value NUMERIC(15,6),
    min_value NUMERIC(15,6),
    max_value NUMERIC(15,6),
    std_dev NUMERIC(15,6),
    
    -- Compliance
    within_threshold_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    outside_threshold_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    compliance_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    
    -- Tendências
    week_over_week_change NUMERIC(10,6),
    rolling_avg_7d NUMERIC(15,6),
    rolling_std_7d NUMERIC(15,6),
    
    -- Alertas
    alert_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    critical_alert_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    PRIMARY KEY (date, metric_category, metric_name)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_quality_trends IS 'Daily quality trends for LLM Specialist analysis';

-- ============================================
-- 4.4 MART OPERACIONAL (SRE)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_operational_health (
    minute TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Disponibilidade
    total_executions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    successful_executions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    availability_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    
    -- Performance
    avg_response_time_ms NUMERIC(10,2),
    error_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    timeout_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Resource health
    avg_cpu_utilization NUMERIC(5,2),
    avg_memory_utilization NUMERIC(5,2),
    peak_concurrent_executions INTEGER,
    
    -- SLA compliance
    sla_violations INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    sla_compliance_rate NUMERIC(5,2),
    
    -- Incident tracking
    incident_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    mttr_minutes NUMERIC(10,2),
    
    PRIMARY KEY (minute)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE diyapp_v10.mart_operational_health IS 'Minute-level operational health metrics for SRE';

-- ============================================
-- 5. ÍNDICES PARA PERFORMANCE

-- Índices para raw tables
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_projects_created ON diyapp_v10.raw_projects(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_executions_project_time ON diyapp_v10.raw_executions(project_id, start_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_executions_status_time ON diyapp_v10.raw_executions(execution_status, start_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_metrics_execution ON diyapp_v10.raw_quality_metrics(execution_id, measured_at);

-- Índices para staging tables
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_projects_active ON diyapp_v10.stg_projects(is_active, created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_executions_time ON diyapp_v10.stg_executions(start_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_executions_project_status ON diyapp_v10.stg_executions(project_id, execution_status);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_metrics_category ON diyapp_v10.stg_quality_metrics(metric_category, measured_at);

-- Índices para mart tables
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_project_date ON diyapp_v10.mart_project_metrics(date);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_project_type ON diyapp_v10.mart_project_metrics(project_type, date);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_execution_hour ON diyapp_v10.mart_execution_analytics(hour);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_quality_date ON diyapp_v10.mart_quality_trends(date);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_ops_minute ON diyapp_v10.mart_operational_health(minute);

-- ============================================
-- 6. VIEWS PARA CONSUMO
-- ============================================

-- View para dashboard do PM
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW diyapp_v10.vw_pm_dashboard AS
SELECT 
    date,
    project_type,
    COUNT(DISTINCT project_id) as active_projects,
    SUM(execution_count) as total_executions,
    AVG(success_rate) as avg_success_rate,
    SUM(critical_issues_count) as total_critical_issues,
    SUM(total_cpu_seconds) / 3600 as total_cpu_hours
FROM diyapp_v10.mart_project_metrics
GROUP BY date, project_type;

-- View para AI Ops (custo e performance)
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW diyapp_v10.vw_aiops_monitoring AS
SELECT 
    date_trunc('hour', hour) as hour,
    execution_type,
    SUM(execution_count) as executions,
    AVG(success_rate) as success_rate,
    AVG(avg_duration_ms) as avg_duration,
    SUM(total_cpu_hours) as cpu_hours,
    SUM(estimated_cost_usd) as estimated_cost
FROM diyapp_v10.mart_execution_analytics
GROUP BY date_trunc('hour', hour), execution_type;

-- View para Especialista LLM (qualidade)
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW diyapp_v10.vw_llm_quality AS
SELECT 
    date,
    metric_category,
    metric_name,
    sample_count,
    avg_value,
    compliance_rate,
    week_over_week_change,
    alert_count
FROM diyapp_v10.mart_quality_trends
WHERE metric_category IN ('code_quality', 'model_performance', 'response_quality');

-- View para SRE (operacional)
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW diyapp_v10.vw_sre_health AS
SELECT 
    date_trunc('minute', minute) as minute,
    availability_rate,
    avg_response_time_ms,
    error_rate,
    avg_cpu_utilization,
    sla_compliance_rate
FROM diyapp_v10.mart_operational_health;

-- ============================================
-- 8. ORQUESTRAÇÃO (Airflow DAG)

-- dag_diyapp_metrics_pipeline.py
"""
DIYAPP Metrics Pipeline DAG
Schedule: Hourly for executions, Daily for projects
"""

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from airflow import DAG
from airflow.operators.python import PythonOperator
from airflow.providers.postgres.operators.postgres import PostgresOperator

default_args = {
    'owner': 'data_engineer',
    'depends_on_past': False,
    'start_date': datetime(2024, 1, 1),
    'email_on_failure': True,
    'email_on_retry': False,
    'retries': 3,
    'retry_delay': timedelta(minutes=5),
}

dag = DAG(
    'diyapp_metrics_pipeline',
    default_args=default_args,
    description='DIYAPP project and execution metrics pipeline',
    schedule_interval='0 * * * *',  # Hourly
    catchup=False,
    tags=['diyapp', 'metrics', 'v10']
)

# Task 1: Ingest raw data
ingest_raw_data = PostgresOperator(
    task_id='ingest_raw_data',
    postgres_conn_id='diyapp_postgres',
    sql='''
    -- Ingest from API to raw tables
    INSERT INTO diyapp_v10.raw_projects (...)
    SELECT ... FROM external.projects_api;
    
    INSERT INTO diyapp_v10.raw_executions (...)
    SELECT ... FROM external.executions_log;
    ''',
    dag=dag
)

# Task 2: Transform to staging
transform_to_staging = PostgresOperator(
    task_id='transform_to_staging',
    postgres_conn_id='diyapp_postgres',
    sql='''
    -- Clean and standardize data
    INSERT INTO diyapp_v10.stg_projects
    SELECT 
        project_id,
        TRIM(project_name),
        CASE 
            WHEN project_config->>'type' IS NOT NULL 
            THEN project_config->>'type'
            ELSE 'unknown'
        END as project_type,
        -- ... other transformations
    FROM diyapp_v10.raw_projects
    WHERE ingestion_timestamp >= NOW() - INTERVAL '1 hour';
    ''',
    dag=dag
)

# Task 3: Run dbt models (via BashOperator or dbtCloudOperator)
run_dbt_models = BashOperator(
    task_id='run_dbt_models',
    bash_command='cd /opt/airflow/dbt/diyapp && dbt run --models marts',
    dag=dag
)

# Task 4: Data quality checks
data_quality_check = PythonOperator(
    task_id='data_quality_check',
    python_callable=run_data_quality_tests,
    dag=dag
)

# Task 5: Update data catalog
update_catalog = PostgresOperator(
    task_id='update_catalog',
    postgres_conn_id='diyapp_postgres',
    sql='''
    -- Update DataHub or internal catalog
    SELECT diyapp_v10.update_data_catalog();


### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
```javascript
// ============================================
// DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
// Módulo de Segurança: Autenticação JWT & Sanitização
// ============================================

// Estrutura de pastas:
// src/
//   security/
//     auth/
//       jwt-service.js
//       middleware.js
//     sanitization/
//       input-sanitizer.js
//       xss-protector.js
//   services/
//     file-permission-service.js
//   app.js
//   server.js
// public/
//   index.html (dashboard de segurança)
// logs/
//   security.log
// .env
// package.json

// ============================================
// 1. package.json (dependências de segurança)
// ============================================

{
  "name": "diyapp-v10-security-core",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "DIYAPP V10 - Módulo de Segurança com JWT e Sanitização",
  "main": "src/server.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/server.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/server.js",
    "test": "jest --coverage",
    "audit": "npm audit --production",
    "snyk-test": "snyk test"
  },
  "dependencies": {
    "express": "^4.18.2",
    "jsonwebtoken": "^9.0.2",
    "bcryptjs": "^2.4.3",
    "helmet": "^7.1.0",
    "express-rate-limit": "^7.1.5",
    "express-validator": "^7.0.1",
    "xss-clean": "^0.1.4",
    "sqlite3": "^5.1.6",
    "winston": "^3.11.0",
    "dotenv": "^16.3.1",
    "cors": "^2.8.5",
    "express-jwt": "^8.4.1",
    "jwks-rsa": "^3.0.1"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "nodemon": "^3.0.1",
    "jest": "^29.7.0",
    "supertest": "^6.3.3",
    "snyk": "^1.1198.0"
  },
  "engines": {
    "node": ">=18.0.0"
  }
}

// ============================================
// 2. .env (variáveis de ambiente - SEGURANÇA)
// ============================================

# SECURITY CONFIGURATION
NODE_ENV=production
PORT=3000

# JWT CONFIGURATION
JWT_SECRET=your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production-min-32-chars
JWT_ACCESS_EXPIRY=15m
JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRY=7d
JWT_ISSUER=diyapp-v10

# RATE LIMITING
RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS=900000
RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS=100

# DATABASE
DB_PATH=./database/security.db

# CORS
ALLOWED_ORIGINS=https://app.diyapp.com,http://localhost:3000

# LOGGING
LOG_LEVEL=info
LOG_SECURITY_EVENTS=true

// ============================================
// 3. src/security/auth/jwt-service.js
// ============================================

const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const winston = require('winston');

class JWTSecurityService {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;
    this.accessExpiry = process.env.JWT_ACCESS_EXPIRY || '15m';
    this.refreshExpiry = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRY || '7d';
    this.issuer = process.env.JWT_ISSUER || 'diyapp-v10';
    
    if (!this.secret || this.secret.length < 32) {
      throw new Error('JWT_SECRET must be at least 32 characters long');
    }
    
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: 'info',
      format: winston.format.json(),
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/security.log' }),
        new winston.transports.Console()
      ]
    });
    
    // In-memory token blacklist (em produção, usar Redis)
    this.tokenBlacklist = new Set();
  }

  /**
   * Gera token de acesso JWT
   * @param {Object} payload - Dados do usuário
   * @returns {String} Token JWT
   */
  generateAccessToken(payload) {
    const tokenPayload = {
      ...payload,
      type: 'access',
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex') // Unique JWT ID
    };

    return jwt.sign(tokenPayload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: this.accessExpiry,
      issuer: this.issuer,
      algorithm: 'HS256'
    });
  }

  /**
   * Gera token de refresh JWT
   * @param {Object} payload - Dados do usuário
   * @returns {String} Token JWT
   */
  generateRefreshToken(payload) {
    const tokenPayload = {
      ...payload,
      type: 'refresh',
      jti: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex')
    };

    return jwt.sign(tokenPayload, this.secret, {
      expiresIn: this.refreshExpiry,
      issuer: this.issuer,
      algorithm: 'HS256'
    });
  }

  /**
   * Verifica e decodifica token JWT
   * @param {String} token - Token JWT
   * @returns {Object} Payload decodificado
   */
  verifyToken(token) {
    try {
      // Verifica se token está na blacklist
      if (this.tokenBlacklist.has(token)) {
        throw new Error('Token revoked');
      }

      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.secret, {
        issuer: this.issuer,
        algorithms: ['HS256']
      });

      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('JWT verification failed', {
        error: error.message,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Revoga token (adiciona à blacklist)
   * @param {String} token - Token a ser revogado
   */
  revokeToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
      if (decoded && decoded.exp) {
        const ttl = decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
        if (ttl > 0) {
          this.tokenBlacklist.add(token);
          
          // Remove da blacklist após expiração
          setTimeout(() => {
            this.tokenBlacklist.delete(token);
          }, ttl * 1000);
          
          this.logger.info('Token revoked', {
            jti: decoded.jti,
            userId: decoded.userId,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
          });
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      this.logger.error('Token revocation failed', {
        error: error.message
      });
    }
  }

  /**
   * Rotaciona tokens (refresh token flow)
   * @param {String} refreshToken - Refresh token atual
   * @returns {Object} Novos tokens
   */
  rotateTokens(refreshToken) {
    const decoded = this.verifyToken(refreshToken);
    
    if (decoded.type !== 'refresh') {
      throw new Error('Invalid token type');
    }

    // Revoga o refresh token antigo
    this.revokeToken(refreshToken);

    // Remove propriedades específicas do token
    const { exp, iat, jti, type, ...userPayload } = decoded;

    // Gera novos tokens
    const newAccessToken = this.generateAccessToken(userPayload);
    const newRefreshToken = this.generateRefreshToken(userPayload);

    return {
      accessToken: newAccessToken,
      refreshToken: newRefreshToken
    };
  }

  /**
   * Valida permissões no token
   * @param {Object} tokenPayload - Payload do token
   * @param {Array} requiredPermissions - Permissões requeridas
   * @returns {Boolean}
   */
  validatePermissions(tokenPayload, requiredPermissions) {
    if (!tokenPayload.permissions || !Array.isArray(tokenPayload.permissions)) {
      return false;
    }

    return requiredPermissions.every(permission => 
      tokenPayload.permissions.includes(permission)
    );
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTSecurityService();

// ============================================
// 4. src/security/auth/middleware.js
// ============================================

const jwtService = require('./jwt-service');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const helmet = require('helmet');

class SecurityMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.rateLimiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS) || 15 * 60 * 1000,
      max: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS) || 100,
      message: {
        error: 'Too many requests',
        retryAfter: '15 minutes'
      },
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false
    });
  }

  /**
   * Middleware de autenticação JWT
   */
  authenticateJWT(req, res, next) {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Authentication required',
        code: 'AUTH_HEADER_MISSING'
      });
    }

    const token = authHeader.substring(7);

    try {
      const decoded = jwtService.verifyToken(token);
      
      // Verifica se é token de acesso
      if (decoded.type !== 'access') {
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Invalid token type',
          code: 'INVALID_TOKEN_TYPE'
        });
      }

      // Adiciona usuário ao request
      req.user = {
        id: decoded.userId,
        email: decoded.email,
        permissions: decoded.permissions || [],
        role: decoded.role
      };

      // Log de acesso bem-sucedido
      req.logger.info('JWT authentication successful', {
        userId: decoded.userId,
        path: req.path,
        method: req.method,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });

      next();
    } catch (error) {
      req.logger.warn('JWT authentication failed', {
        error: error.message,
        path: req.path,
        ip: req.ip,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });

      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Invalid or expired token',
        code: 'INVALID_TOKEN'
      });
    }
  }

  /**
   * Middleware de autorização baseada em permissões
   * @param {Array} requiredPermissions - Permissões requeridas
   */
  authorize(requiredPermissions = []) {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      if (!req.user) {
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Authentication required',
          code: 'UNAUTHORIZED'
        });
      }

      const hasPermission = jwtService.validatePermissions(
        req.user,
        requiredPermissions
      );

      if (!hasPermission) {
        req.logger.warn('Authorization failed', {
          userId: req.user.id,
          requiredPermissions,
          userPermissions: req.user.permissions,
          path: req.path,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });

        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Insufficient permissions',
          code: 'FORBIDDEN'
        });
      }

      next();
    };
  }

  /**
   * Middleware de rate limiting
   */
  getRateLimiter() {
    return this.rateLimiter;
  }

  /**
   * Middleware de segurança HTTP (Helmet)
   */
  getSecurityHeaders() {
    return helmet({
      contentSecurityPolicy: {
        directives: {
          defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
          styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
          scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
          imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
          connectSrc: ["'self'"],
          fontSrc: ["'self'"],
          objectSrc: ["'none'"],
          mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
          frameSrc: ["'none'"]
        }
      },
      hsts: {
        maxAge: 31536000,
        includeSubDomains: true,
        preload: true
      },
      referrerPolicy: { policy: 'strict-origin-when-cross-origin' }
    });
  }

  /**
   * Middleware de CORS seguro
   */
  getCorsMiddleware() {
    const cors = require('cors');
    const allowedOrigins = process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS 
      ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') 
      : [];

    return cors({
      origin: (origin, callback) => {
        // Permite requests sem origin (mobile apps, curl, etc)
        if (!origin) return callback(null, true);
        
        if (allowedOrigins.indexOf(origin) === -1) {
          const msg = 'The CORS policy for this site does not allow access from the specified Origin.';
          return callback(new Error(msg), false);
        }
        return callback(null, true);
      },
      credentials: true,
      methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
      allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Request-ID']
    });
  }

  /**
   * Middleware de logging de segurança
   */
  securityLogger(req, res, next) {
    req.logger = require('winston').child({
      service: 'security',
      requestId: crypto.randomBytes(8).toString('hex'),
      ip: req.ip,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent')
    });

    // Log de request
    req.logger.info('Request received', {
      method: req.method,
      path: req.path,
      query: req.query,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });

    // Intercepta response para logging
    const originalSend = res.send;
    res.send = function(data) {
      // Log de response
      req.logger.info('Response sent', {
        statusCode: res.statusCode,
        path: req.path,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });

      if (res.statusCode >= 400) {
        req.logger.warn('Error response', {
          statusCode: res.statusCode,
          path: req.path,
          error: data.error,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      }

      originalSend.call(this, data);
    };

    next();
  }
}

module.exports = new SecurityMiddleware();

// ============================================
// 5. src/security/sanitization/input-sanitizer.js
// ============================================

const { body, query, param, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const xss = require('xss-clean');
const winston = require('winston');

class InputSanitizer {
  constructor() {
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: 'info',
      format: winston.format.json(),
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/sanitization.log' })
      ]
    });
  }

  /**
   * Sanitiza strings contra XSS
   * @param {String} input - Input a ser sanitizado
   * @returns {String} Input sanitizado
   */
  sanitizeString(input) {
    if (typeof input !== 'string') return input;
    
    // Remove null bytes
    let sanitized = input.replace(/\0/g, '');
    
    // Remove caracteres de controle (exceto tab, newline, carriage return)
    sanitized = sanitized.replace(/[\x00-\x08\x0B\x0C\x0E-\x1F\x7F]/g, '');
    
    // Trim whitespace
    sanitized = sanitized.trim();
    
    // Limita tamanho máximo (prevenção de DoS)
    if (sanitized.length > 10000) {
      sanitized = sanitized.substring(0, 10000);
      this.logger.warn('Input truncated due to length', {
        originalLength: input.length,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
    
    return sanitized;
  }

  /**
   * Sanitiza objeto completo recursivamente
   * @param {Object} obj - Objeto a ser sanitizado
   * @returns {Object} Objeto sanitizado
   */
  sanitizeObject(obj) {
    if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return obj;
    
    const sanitized = Array.isArray(obj) ? [] : {};
    
    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
      if (typeof value === 'string') {
        sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeString(value);
      } else if (typeof value === 'object' && value !== null) {
        sanitized[key] = this.sanitizeObject(value);
      } else {
        sanitized[key] = value;
      }
    }
    
    return sanitized;
  }

  /**
   * Validação para login
   */
  getLoginValidation() {
    return [
      body('email')
        .isEmail().normalizeEmail()
        .withMessage('Invalid email address'),
      body('password')
        .isLength({ min: 8 })
        .withMessage('Password must be at least 8 characters')
        .matches(/[A-Z]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one uppercase letter')
        .matches(/[a-z]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one lowercase letter')
        .matches(/\d/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one number')
        .matches(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/).withMessage('Password must contain at least one special character'),
      this.handleValidationErrors
    ];
  }

  /**
   * Validação para criação de usuário
   */
  getUserCreationValidation() {
    return [
      body('email')
        .isEmail().normalizeEmail()
        .withMessage('Invalid email

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]

// Comandos customizados do Cypress
import './commands'

// Hooks globais
beforeEach(() => {
  // Limpar localStorage e sessionStorage
  cy.clearLocalStorage()
  cy.clearCookies()
  
  // Log do teste atual
  cy.log(`Running test: ${Cypress.currentTest.title}`)
})

afterEach(() => {
  // Capturar screenshot em caso de falha
  if (Cypress.currentTest.state === 'failed') {
    const screenshotName = `${Cypress.currentTest.titlePath.join(' -- ')} (failed)`
    cy.screenshot(screenshotName, { overwrite: true })
  }
})

// Interceptar e logar requisições de API
Cypress.on('window:before:load', (win) => {
  cy.spy(win.console, 'error')
  cy.spy(win.console, 'warn')
})

afterEach(() => {
  cy.window().then((win) => {
    if (win.console.error.called) {
      cy.log('Console errors detected:', win.console.error.getCalls())
    }
  })
})

// Comando para login de teste
Cypress.Commands.add('login', (email, password) => {
  email = email || Cypress.env('TEST_USER_EMAIL')
  password = password || Cypress.env('TEST_USER_PASSWORD')
  
  cy.session([email, password], () => {
    cy.visit('/login')
    cy.get('[data-cy="email-input"]').type(email)
    cy.get('[data-cy="password-input"]').type(password)
    cy.get('[data-cy="login-button"]').click()
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard')
    cy.get('[data-cy="user-menu"]').should('be.visible')
  }, {
    cacheAcrossSpecs: true
  })
})

// Comando para criar agente de teste
Cypress.Commands.add('createTestAgent', (agentData = {}) => {
  const defaultAgent = {
    name: `Test Agent ${Date.now()}`,
    role: 'developer',
    capabilities: ['code', 'test'],
    config: { temperature: 0.7 }
  }
  
  const agent = { ...defaultAgent, ...agentData }
  
  return cy.request({
    method: 'POST',
    url: `${Cypress.env('API_URL')}/agents`,
    headers: {
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
    },
    body: agent
  }).then((response) => {
    expect(response.status).to.eq(201)
    return response.body
  })
})

// Comando para testar comunicação entre agentes
Cypress.Commands.add('testAgentCommunication', (senderId, receiverId, message) => {
  return cy.request({
    method: 'POST',
    url: `${Cypress.env('API_URL')}/agents/${senderId}/communicate`,
    headers: {
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`
    },
    body: {
      receiverId,
      message,
      channel: 'direct'
    }
  })
})

// Comando para validar output de LLM
Cypress.Commands.add('validateLLMOutput', (prompt, expectedCriteria) => {
  return cy.request({
    method: 'POST',
    url: `${Cypress.env('API_URL')}/llm/generate`,
    headers: {
      'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('token')}`,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    body: {
      prompt,
      temperature: 0.7,
      maxTokens: 500
    }
  }).then((response) => {
    expect(response.status).to.eq(200)
    
    // Validar critérios
    const output = response.body.output
    
    if (expectedCriteria.format) {
      expect(output).to.match(new RegExp(expectedCriteria.format))
    }
    
    if (expectedCriteria.contains) {
      expectedCriteria.contains.forEach(term => {
        expect(output.toLowerCase()).to.include(term.toLowerCase())
      })
    }
    
    if (expectedCriteria.notContains) {
      expectedCriteria.notContains.forEach(term => {
        expect(output.toLowerCase()).not.to.include(term.toLowerCase())
      })
    }
    
    if (expectedCriteria.maxLength) {
      expect(output.length).to.be.lessThan(expectedCriteria.maxLength)
    }
    
    return response.body
  })
})
```

### `tests/e2e/cypress/integration/agent-communication.cy.js`

```javascript
describe('Comunicação entre Agentes - Fluxos E2E', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.login()
    cy.visit('/agents')
  })

  describe('Cenário 1: Comunicação Direta entre Agentes', () => {
    it('Deve permitir que um agente desenvolvedor envie tarefa para um agente QA', () => {
      // Criar agentes de teste
      cy.createTestAgent({
        name: 'Dev Agent',
        role: 'developer',
        capabilities: ['code', 'refactor']
      }).then((devAgent) => {
        cy.createTestAgent({
          name: 'QA Agent',
          role: 'qa',
          capabilities: ['test', 'validate']
        }).then((qaAgent) => {
          // Navegar para comunicação
          cy.visit(`/agents/${devAgent.id}/communicate`)
          
          // Selecionar agente QA como destinatário
          cy.get('[data-cy="receiver-select"]').select(qaAgent.id)
          
          // Enviar mensagem de tarefa
          const taskMessage = 'Implementar testes para o módulo de autenticação'
          cy.get('[data-cy="message-input"]').type(taskMessage)
          cy.get('[data-cy="send-button"]').click()
          
          // Verificar confirmação
          cy.get('[data-cy="message-sent"]').should('be.visible')
          cy.get('[data-cy="message-content"]').should('contain', taskMessage)
          
          // Verificar que o agente QA recebeu a mensagem
          cy.visit(`/agents/${qaAgent.id}/inbox`)
          cy.get('[data-cy="inbox-message"]').should('contain', taskMessage)
          cy.get('[data-cy="message-sender"]').should('contain', devAgent.name)
        })
      })
    })

    it('Deve processar resposta do agente QA com aceitação da tarefa', () => {
      cy.createTestAgent({
        name: 'QA Agent',
        role: 'qa',
        capabilities: ['test', 'validate']
      }).then((qaAgent) => {
        cy.visit(`/agents/${qaAgent.id}/inbox`)
        
        // Simular mensagem recebida
        cy.get('[data-cy="simulate-message"]').click()
        cy.get('[data-cy="simulate-sender"]').type('Dev Agent')
        cy.get('[data-cy="simulate-content"]').type('Implementar testes E2E para checkout')
        cy.get('[data-cy="simulate-send"]').click()
        
        // Responder à mensagem
        cy.get('[data-cy="reply-button"]').first().click()
        cy.get('[data-cy="reply-input"]').type('Tarefa aceita. Iniciando implementação dos testes.')
        cy.get('[data-cy="reply-send"]').click()
        
        // Verificar resposta enviada
        cy.get('[data-cy="reply-sent"]').should('be.visible')
        cy.get('[data-cy="task-status"]').should('contain', 'accepted')
      })
    })
  })

  describe('Cenário 2: Comunicação em Grupo (Squad)', () => {
    it('Deve criar sala de squad e permitir comunicação entre todos os membros', () => {
      // Criar squad de teste
      cy.get('[data-cy="create-squad"]').click()
      cy.get('[data-cy="squad-name"]').type('Squad Autônoma V10')
      cy.get('[data-cy="squad-description"]').type('Squad para testes de comunicação')
      
      // Adicionar agentes à squad
      cy.createTestAgent({ name: 'Product Owner', role: 'po' }).then((poAgent) => {
        cy.createTestAgent({ name: 'Tech Lead', role: 'tech_lead' }).then((tlAgent) => {
          cy.get('[data-cy="add-agent"]').select(poAgent.id)
          cy.get('[data-cy="add-agent-button"]').click()
          cy.get('[data-cy="add-agent"]').select(tlAgent.id)
          cy.get('[data-cy="add-agent-button"]').click()
          
          cy.get('[data-cy="save-squad"]').click()
          
          // Verificar squad criada
          cy.get('[data-cy="squad-created"]').should('be.visible')
          cy.get('[data-cy="squad-members"]').should('contain', '2 membros')
          
          // Enviar mensagem para a squad
          cy.get('[data-cy="squad-chat-input"]').type('Daily standup iniciada. Todos reportem status.')
          cy.get('[data-cy="squad-send"]').click()
          
          // Verificar mensagem enviada para todos
          cy.get('[data-cy="squad-message"]').should('have.length.at.least', 2)
        })
      })
    })

    it('Deve processar respostas de múltiplos agentes na squad', () => {
      cy.visit('/squads')
      cy.get('[data-cy="squad-item"]').first().click()
      
      // Simular respostas dos agentes
      cy.get('[data-cy="simulate-agent-response"]').click()
      cy.get('[data-cy="response-agent"]').select('Product Owner')
      cy.get('[data-cy="response-content"]').type('Implementando user stories de checkout')
      cy.get('[data-cy="add-response"]').click()
      
      cy.get('[data-cy="response-agent"]').select('Tech Lead')
      cy.get('[data-cy="response-content"]').type('Revisando arquitetura do módulo de pagamento')
      cy.get('[data-cy="add-response"]').click()
      
      // Verificar histórico de comunicação
      cy.get('[data-cy="chat-history"]').should('contain', 'Product Owner')
      cy.get('[data-cy="chat-history"]').should('contain', 'Tech Lead')
      cy.get('[data-cy="communication-summary"]').should('contain', '2 respostas')
    })
  })

  describe('Cenário 3: Comunicação Assíncrona com Retry', () => {
    it('Deve lidar com falha de comunicação e tentar novamente', () => {
      cy.createTestAgent({
        name: 'Unresponsive Agent',
        role: 'developer',
        config: { responseTimeout: 1000 }
      }).then((agent) => {
        cy.visit(`/agents/${agent.id}/communicate`)
        
        // Configurar cenário de falha
        cy.get('[data-cy="simulate-failure"]').click()
        cy.get('[data-cy="failure-type"]').select('timeout')
        cy.get('[data-cy="apply-failure"]').click()
        
        // Tentar enviar mensagem
        cy.get('[data-cy="message-input"]').type('Teste de timeout')
        cy.get('[data-cy="send-button"]').click()
        
        // Verificar tentativas de retry
        cy.get('[data-cy="retry-attempt"]', { timeout: 10000 }).should('be.visible')
        cy.get('[data-cy="retry-count"]').should('contain', '3')
        
        // Verificar fallback após retries
        cy.get('[data-cy="fallback-action"]').should('be.visible')
        cy.get('[data-cy="message-queued"]').should('contain', 'mensagem na fila')
      })
    })

    it('Deve processar mensagens da fila quando o agente voltar', () => {
      cy.createTestAgent({ name: 'Recovered Agent', role: 'developer' }).then((agent) => {
        cy.visit(`/agents/${agent.id}/queue`)
        
        // Adicionar mensagens à fila
        cy.get('[data-cy="add-queued-message"]').click()
        cy.get('[data-cy="queued-content"]').type('Mensagem 1 da fila')
        cy.get('[data-cy="save-queued"]').click()
        
        cy.get('[data-cy="add-queued-message"]').click()
        cy.get('[data-cy="queued-content"]').type('Mensagem 2 da fila')
        cy.get('[data-cy="save-queued"]').click()
        
        // Processar fila
        cy.get('[data-cy="process-queue"]').click()
        
        // Verificar processamento
        cy.get('[data-cy="queue-processing"]', { timeout: 5000 }).should('be.visible')
        cy.get('[data-cy="queue-empty"]', { timeout: 10000 }).should('be.visible')
        cy.get('[data-cy="processed-count"]').should('contain', '2')
      })
    })
  })

  describe('Cenário 4: Validação de Protocolos de Comunicação', () => {
    it('Deve validar formato das mensagens entre agentes', () => {
      cy.createTestAgent({ name: 'Validator Agent', role: 'qa' }).then((agent) => {
        cy.visit(`/agents/${agent.id}/validate`)
        
        // Testar mensagem válida
        const validMessage = {
          sender: 'dev-agent-001',
          receiver: 'qa-agent-001',
          message: 'Implementar testes unitários',
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          metadata: { priority: 'high', type: 'task' }
        }
        
        cy.get('[data-cy="message-json"]').type(JSON.stringify(validMessage, null, 2))
        cy.get('[data-cy="validate-format"]').click()
        
        cy.get('[data-cy="validation-result"]').should('contain', 'válida')
        cy.get('[data-cy="required-fields"]').should('contain', '5/5')
        
        // Testar mensagem inválida
        const invalidMessage = {
          sender: 'dev-agent-001',
          // receiver faltando
          message: 'Teste'
        }
        
        cy.get('[data-cy="message-json"]').clear().type(JSON.stringify(invalidMessage))
        cy.get('[data-cy="validate-format"]').click()
        
        cy.get('[data-cy="validation-result"]').should('contain', 'inválida')
        cy.get('[data-cy="missing-fields"]').should('contain', 'receiver')
      })
    })

    it('Deve aplicar sanitização em mensagens maliciosas', () => {
      cy.visit('/agents/security-test')
      
      const maliciousMessages = [
        '<script>alert
