## 1. Documentação da API (OpenAPI/Swagger)

### `docs/api/openapi.yaml`
```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: DIYAPP Evolution V10 Core API
  description: API para o sistema autônomo DIYAPP Evolution V10
  version: 10.0.0
  contact:
    name: Squad Autônoma DIYAPP
    email: devops@diyapp.com
  license:
    name: Proprietary
    url: https://diyapp.com/license
servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp.com/v10
    description: Production server
  - url: https://staging.api.diyapp.com/v10
    description: Staging server
  - url: http://localhost:3000/v10
    description: Local development

tags:
  - name: Authentication
    description: Autenticação e autorização
  - name: Agents
    description: Gerenciamento de agentes autônomos
  - name: Tasks
    description: Gerenciamento de tarefas e workflows
  - name: Monitoring
    description: Monitoramento e métricas
  - name: System
    description: Operações do sistema

paths:
  /auth/token:
    post:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: Obter token de acesso
      description: Autentica um agente ou usuário e retorna um token JWT
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token gerado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'

  /agents:
    get:
      tags: [Agents]
      summary: Listar agentes ativos
      description: Retorna lista de todos os agentes autônomos em execução
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, idle, error]
          description: Filtrar por status
        - name: type
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [writer, developer, sre, compliance, innovation]
          description: Filtrar por tipo de agente
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de agentes
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: array
                items:
                  $ref: '#/components/schemas/Agent'
        '403':
          description: Acesso não autorizado

    post:
      tags: [Agents]
      summary: Criar novo agente
      description: Instancia um novo agente autônomo
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentCreate'
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Agente criado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Agent'
        '400':
          description: Dados inválidos
        '429':
          description: Limite de agentes excedido

  /agents/{agentId}:
    get:
      tags: [Agents]
      summary: Obter detalhes do agente
      description: Retorna informações detalhadas de um agente específico
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: agentId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
          description: ID do agente
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Detalhes do agente
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentDetail'
        '404':
          description: Agente não encontrado

    delete:
      tags: [Agents]
      summary: Encerrar agente
      description: Encerra um agente autônomo de forma segura
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: agentId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
      responses:
        '204':
          description: Agente encerrado com sucesso
        '404':
          description: Agente não encontrado
        '409':
          description: Agente não pode ser encerrado (em tarefa crítica)

  /tasks:
    post:
      tags: [Tasks]
      summary: Criar nova tarefa
      description: Cria uma nova tarefa para execução pelos agentes
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/TaskCreate'
      responses:
        '202':
          description: Tarefa aceita para processamento
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Task'
        '400':
          description: Tarefa inválida

  /tasks/{taskId}:
    get:
      tags: [Tasks]
      summary: Obter status da tarefa
      description: Retorna o status atual de uma tarefa
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: taskId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            format: uuid
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Status da tarefa
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/TaskStatus'
        '404':
          description: Tarefa não encontrada

  /monitoring/metrics:
    get:
      tags: [Monitoring]
      summary: Obter métricas do sistema
      description: Retorna métricas de performance e saúde do sistema
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: timeframe
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [1h, 24h, 7d, 30d]
            default: 1h
          description: Período de tempo para as métricas
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Métricas do sistema
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Metrics'

  /system/health:
    get:
      tags: [System]
      summary: Verificar saúde do sistema
      description: Retorna status de saúde de todos os componentes
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Sistema saudável
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/HealthCheck'
        '503':
          description: Sistema com problemas

components:
  securitySchemes:
    BearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT

  schemas:
    AuthRequest:
      type: object
      required: [agent_id, secret_key]
      properties:
        agent_id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
          example: "123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000"
        secret_key:
          type: string
          format: password
          example: "sk_live_xyz123"
        scope:
          type: array
          items:
            type: string
            enum: [read, write, admin]
          example: ["read", "write"]

    AuthResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        access_token:
          type: string
          example: "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..."
        token_type:
          type: string
          example: "Bearer"
        expires_in:
          type: integer
          example: 3600
        scope:
          type: string
          example: "read write"

    Agent:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
          example: "123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000"
        name:
          type: string
          example: "tech-writer-senior"
        type:
          type: string
          enum: [writer, developer, sre, compliance, innovation]
          example: "writer"
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [active, idle, error, terminated]
          example: "active"
        created_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
          example: "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
        last_heartbeat:
          type: string
          format: date-time
          example: "2024-01-15T14:45:00Z"

    AgentCreate:
      type: object
      required: [name, type, config]
      properties:
        name:
          type: string
          example: "new-tech-writer"
        type:
          type: string
          enum: [writer, developer, sre, compliance, innovation]
          example: "writer"
        config:
          type: object
          properties:
            model:
              type: string
              example: "gpt-4"
            capabilities:
              type: array
              items:
                type: string
              example: ["documentation", "api-spec", "tutorials"]
            memory_limit_mb:
              type: integer
              example: 512

    AgentDetail:
      allOf:
        - $ref: '#/components/schemas/Agent'
        - type: object
          properties:
            current_task:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/TaskReference'
            performance_metrics:
              type: object
              properties:
                tasks_completed:
                  type: integer
                  example: 42
                avg_execution_time_ms:
                  type: integer
                  example: 1250
                error_rate:
                  type: number
                  format: float
                  example: 0.02
            config:
              type: object

    TaskCreate:
      type: object
      required: [type, priority, payload]
      properties:
        type:
          type: string
          enum: [documentation, development, monitoring, compliance, innovation]
          example: "documentation"
        priority:
          type: string
          enum: [low, medium, high, critical]
          example: "high"
        payload:
          type: object
          properties:
            title:
              type: string
              example: "Document API endpoints"
            description:
              type: string
              example: "Create OpenAPI documentation for new endpoints"
            requirements:
              type: array
              items:
                type: string
              example: ["swagger", "examples", "error-codes"]
        assigned_to:
          type: string
          format: uuid
          example: "123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000"

    Task:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
          example: "123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174001"
        type:
          type: string
        priority:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [pending, assigned, in_progress, completed, failed]
          example: "pending"
        created_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        assigned_to:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        estimated_completion:
          type: string
          format: date-time

    TaskStatus:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        status:
          type: string
        progress:
          type: integer
          minimum: 0
          maximum: 100
          example: 75
        result:
          type: object
        error:
          type: string
        updated_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time

    TaskReference:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          format: uuid
        title:
          type: string
        status:
          type: string

    Metrics:
      type: object
      properties:
        system:
          type: object
          properties:
            uptime:
              type: number
              format: float
              example: 99.95
            active_agents:
              type: integer
              example: 15
            cpu_usage_percent:
              type: number
              format: float
              example: 45.2
            memory_usage_percent:
              type: number
              format: float
              example: 67.8
        tasks:
          type: object
          properties:
            completed_last_hour:
              type: integer
              example: 42
            failed_last_hour:
              type: integer
              example: 2
            avg_completion_time_ms:
              type: integer
              example: 2300
        agents:
          type: object
          additionalProperties:
            type: object
            properties:
              active:
                type: integer
              idle:
                type: integer
              error:
                type: integer

    HealthCheck:
      type: object
      properties:
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [healthy, degraded, unhealthy]
          example: "healthy"
        timestamp:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        components:
          type: array
          items:
            type: object
            properties:
              name:
                type: string
                example: "database"
              status:
                type: string
                enum: [up, down, slow]
              response_time_ms:
                type: integer
              last_check:
                  type: string
                  format: date-time

    Error:
      type: object
      properties:
        error:
          type: string
          example: "invalid_credentials"
        message:
          type: string
          example: "The provided credentials are invalid"
        details:
          type: object
        timestamp:
          type: string
          format: date-time
```

### `docs/api/api-guide.md`
```markdown
# Guia da API - DIYAPP Evolution V10

**Data de criação:** 2024-01-15  
**Última atualização:** 2024-01-15  
**Owner:** Tech Writer Senior  
**Versão da API:** 10.0.0

## Visão Geral

A API V10 do DIYAPP Evolution permite a interação programática com o sistema autônomo de agentes. Esta API é RESTful, utiliza JSON para comunicação e autenticação via JWT.

## Autenticação

### 1. Obter Token de Acesso

**Endpoint:** `POST /auth/token`

```bash
curl -X POST https://api.diyapp.com/v10/auth/token \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "agent_id": "123e4567-e89b-12d3-a456-426614174000",
    "secret_key": "sua_chave_secreta",
    "scope": ["read", "write"]
  }'
```

**Resposta de sucesso:**
```json
{
  "access_token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
  "token_type": "Bearer",
  "expires_in": 3600,
  "scope": "read write"
}
```

### 2. Usar o Token

Inclua o token no header `Authorization`:

```bash
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9..." \
  https://api.diyapp.com/v10/agents
```

## Guia de Integração Rápida

### Passo 1: Configurar Ambiente

```javascript
// Exemplo em Node.js
const DIYAPP_API = {
  baseURL: 'https://api.diyapp.com/v10',
  async getToken(agentId, secretKey) {
    const response = await fetch(`${this.baseURL}/auth/token`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ agent_id: agentId, secret_key: secretKey })
    });
    return response.json();
  },
  
  async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
    const token = await this.getToken();
    return fetch(`${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`, {
      ...options,
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${token.access_token}`,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        ...options.headers
      }
    });
  }
};
```

### Passo 2: Gerenciar Agentes

**Listar agentes ativos:**
```bash
curl -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN" \
  "https://api.diyapp.com/v10/agents?status=active&type=writer"
```

**Criar novo agente:**
```bash
curl -X POST https://api.diyapp.com/v10/agents \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "name": "meu-tech-writer",
    "type": "writer",
    "config": {
      "model": "gpt-4",
      "capabilities": ["documentation", "api-spec"],
      "memory_limit_mb": 512
    }
  }'
```

### Passo 3: Criar Tarefas

```bash
curl -X POST https://api.diyapp.com/v10/tasks \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer TOKEN" \
  -H

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]

            height: 300px;
            width: 100%;
        }
        
        .status-indicator {
            width: 12px;
            height: 12px;
            border-radius: 50%;
            display: inline-block;
            margin-right: 5px;
        }
        
        .status-healthy { background-color: var(--success-color); }
        .status-warning { background-color: var(--warning-color); }
        .status-critical { background-color: var(--danger-color); }
        
        .nav-link.active {
            background-color: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
            border-left: 4px solid var(--secondary-color);
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container-fluid">

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
-- Data Engineering: PostgreSQL Schema + dbt Models
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 1. SCHEMA: raw (bronze layer - immutable)
-- ============================================
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw;

-- Raw project definitions (from frontend/API)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.projects (
    project_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    project_config JSONB NOT NULL,
    created_by VARCHAR(100),
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'frontend_api',
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Raw execution logs (from execution engine)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.execution_logs (
    execution_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    project_id UUID NOT NULL,
    execution_type VARCHAR(50) CHECK (execution_type IN ('manual', 'scheduled', 'webhook', 'test')),
    status VARCHAR(50) CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'running', 'success', 'failed', 'cancelled')),
    input_data JSONB,
    output_data JSONB,
    error_details TEXT,
    started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    resource_usage JSONB, -- CPU, memory, tokens, cost
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'execution_engine',
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Raw user interactions (from frontend analytics)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.user_interactions (
    interaction_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id VARCHAR(100),
    session_id VARCHAR(100),
    project_id UUID,
    interaction_type VARCHAR(50) CHECK (interaction_type IN ('project_create', 'project_edit', 'execution_run', 'dashboard_view', 'export')),
    interaction_details JSONB,
    browser_info JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'frontend_analytics',
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Raw system metrics (from infrastructure)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw.system_metrics (
    metric_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    metric_type VARCHAR(50) CHECK (metric_type IN ('cpu', 'memory', 'disk', 'network', 'queue_length')),
    metric_value DECIMAL(10,2),
    metric_unit VARCHAR(20),
    node_name VARCHAR(100),
    collected_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    source_system VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'prometheus',
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- ============================================
-- 2. SCHEMA: staging (silver layer - cleaned)
-- ============================================
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging;

-- Staging: projects with cleaned data
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_projects AS
SELECT 
    project_id,
    TRIM(project_name) AS project_name,
    project_config,
    -- Extract config metadata
    COALESCE((project_config->>'version')::VARCHAR, '1.0') AS config_version,
    (project_config->>'isTemplate')::BOOLEAN AS is_template,
    COALESCE((project_config->>'complexityScore')::INTEGER, 0) AS complexity_score,
    -- User info
    COALESCE(created_by, 'anonymous') AS created_by,
    -- Timestamps
    created_at,
    updated_at,
    -- Quality flags
    CASE 
        WHEN project_name IS NULL OR LENGTH(TRIM(project_name)) = 0 THEN FALSE
        WHEN project_config IS NULL THEN FALSE
        ELSE TRUE
    END AS is_valid,
    -- Source tracking
    source_system,
    ingested_at
FROM raw.projects;

-- Staging: execution logs with standardized fields
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_execution_logs AS
SELECT 
    execution_id,
    project_id,
    execution_type,
    status,
    -- Input/output size metrics
    COALESCE(LENGTH(input_data::TEXT), 0) AS input_size_bytes,
    COALESCE(LENGTH(output_data::TEXT), 0) AS output_size_bytes,
    -- Error classification
    CASE 
        WHEN error_details IS NOT NULL THEN 'error'
        WHEN status = 'failed' THEN 'failure'
        ELSE 'success'
    END AS execution_category,
    -- Duration analysis
    duration_ms,
    CASE 
        WHEN duration_ms < 1000 THEN 'fast'
        WHEN duration_ms < 5000 THEN 'medium'
        WHEN duration_ms < 30000 THEN 'slow'
        ELSE 'very_slow'
    END AS duration_category,
    -- Resource extraction
    COALESCE((resource_usage->>'cpu_seconds')::DECIMAL(10,4), 0) AS cpu_seconds,
    COALESCE((resource_usage->>'memory_mb')::DECIMAL(10,2), 0) AS memory_mb,
    COALESCE((resource_usage->>'tokens_used')::INTEGER, 0) AS tokens_used,
    COALESCE((resource_usage->>'estimated_cost_usd')::DECIMAL(10,6), 0) AS estimated_cost_usd,
    -- Timestamps
    started_at,
    completed_at,
    -- Quality flags
    CASE 
        WHEN project_id IS NULL THEN FALSE
        WHEN started_at IS NULL THEN FALSE
        WHEN status NOT IN ('pending', 'running', 'success', 'failed', 'cancelled') THEN FALSE
        ELSE TRUE
    END AS is_valid,
    -- Source tracking
    source_system,
    ingested_at
FROM raw.execution_logs;

-- Staging: user interactions
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_user_interactions AS
SELECT 
    interaction_id,
    COALESCE(user_id, 'anonymous') AS user_id,
    session_id,
    project_id,
    interaction_type,
    -- Extract common details
    COALESCE((interaction_details->>'elementId')::VARCHAR, 'unknown') AS element_id,
    COALESCE((interaction_details->>'action')::VARCHAR, 'unknown') AS action_detail,
    -- Browser info
    COALESCE((browser_info->>'userAgent')::VARCHAR, 'unknown') AS user_agent,
    COALESCE((browser_info->>'language')::VARCHAR, 'unknown') AS browser_language,
    -- Timestamps
    created_at,
    -- Session sequence
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY session_id ORDER BY created_at) AS session_sequence,
    -- Quality flags
    CASE 
        WHEN interaction_type IS NULL THEN FALSE
        WHEN created_at IS NULL THEN FALSE
        ELSE TRUE
    END AS is_valid,
    -- Source tracking
    source_system,
    ingested_at
FROM raw.user_interactions;

-- Staging: system metrics
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging.stg_system_metrics AS
SELECT 
    metric_id,
    metric_type,
    -- Normalize values
    CASE 
        WHEN metric_unit = 'percent' AND metric_value > 100 THEN 100
        WHEN metric_unit = 'percent' AND metric_value < 0 THEN 0
        ELSE metric_value
    END AS metric_value_normalized,
    metric_unit,
    node_name,
    collected_at,
    -- Alert thresholds
    CASE 
        WHEN metric_type = 'cpu' AND metric_value > 80 THEN 'warning'
        WHEN metric_type = 'memory' AND metric_value > 85 THEN 'warning'
        WHEN metric_type = 'disk' AND metric_value > 90 THEN 'warning'
        WHEN metric_type = 'queue_length' AND metric_value > 100 THEN 'warning'
        ELSE 'normal'
    END AS alert_level,
    -- Quality flags
    CASE 
        WHEN metric_value IS NULL THEN FALSE
        WHEN collected_at IS NULL THEN FALSE
        ELSE TRUE
    END AS is_valid,
    -- Source tracking
    source_system,
    ingested_at
FROM raw.system_metrics;

-- ============================================
-- 3. SCHEMA: marts (gold layer - business ready)
-- ============================================
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts;

-- Mart: Project metrics for PM
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.mart_project_metrics AS
SELECT 
    -- Dimensions
    DATE(p.created_at) AS metric_date,
    p.project_id,
    p.project_name,
    p.created_by,
    p.config_version,
    p.complexity_score,
    p.is_template,
    
    -- Usage metrics
    COUNT(DISTINCT e.execution_id) AS total_executions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN e.status = 'success' THEN e.execution_id END) AS successful_executions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN e.status = 'failed' THEN e.execution_id END) AS failed_executions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT u.session_id) AS unique_user_sessions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT u.user_id) AS unique_users,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY e.duration_ms) AS median_duration_ms,
    AVG(e.duration_ms) AS avg_duration_ms,
    MAX(e.duration_ms) AS max_duration_ms,
    
    -- Resource metrics
    SUM(e.tokens_used) AS total_tokens_used,
    SUM(e.estimated_cost_usd) AS total_estimated_cost,
    AVG(e.cpu_seconds) AS avg_cpu_seconds,
    AVG(e.memory_mb) AS avg_memory_mb,
    
    -- Quality metrics
    AVG(CASE WHEN e.status = 'success' THEN 1.0 ELSE 0.0 END) AS success_rate,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN e.error_details IS NOT NULL THEN e.execution_id END) AS error_count,
    
    -- Freshness
    MAX(e.completed_at) AS last_execution_time,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS calculated_at
    
FROM staging.stg_projects p
LEFT JOIN staging.stg_execution_logs e ON p.project_id = e.project_id
LEFT JOIN staging.stg_user_interactions u ON p.project_id = u.project_id
WHERE p.is_valid = TRUE
GROUP BY 
    DATE(p.created_at),
    p.project_id,
    p.project_name,
    p.created_by,
    p.config_version,
    p.complexity_score,
    p.is_template;

-- Mart: Execution analytics for AI Ops
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.mart_execution_analytics AS
SELECT 
    -- Time dimensions
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', e.started_at) AS execution_hour,
    DATE(e.started_at) AS execution_date,
    EXTRACT(HOUR FROM e.started_at) AS hour_of_day,
    
    -- Resource dimensions
    e.execution_type,
    e.duration_category,
    e.project_id,
    
    -- Aggregated metrics
    COUNT(*) AS total_executions,
    SUM(CASE WHEN e.status = 'success' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS successful_executions,
    SUM(CASE WHEN e.status = 'failed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS failed_executions,
    
    -- Cost metrics
    SUM(e.tokens_used) AS total_tokens_used,
    SUM(e.estimated_cost_usd) AS total_cost_usd,
    AVG(e.estimated_cost_usd) AS avg_cost_per_execution,
    
    -- Performance metrics
    AVG(e.duration_ms) AS avg_duration_ms,
    PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY e.duration_ms) AS p95_duration_ms,
    MAX(e.duration_ms) AS max_duration_ms,
    
    -- Error analysis
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN e.error_details IS NOT NULL THEN e.execution_id END) AS error_count,
    
    -- System correlation
    AVG(s.metric_value_normalized) AS avg_system_load
    
FROM staging.stg_execution_logs e
LEFT JOIN staging.stg_system_metrics s 
    ON DATE_TRUNC('minute', e.started_at) = DATE_TRUNC('minute', s.collected_at)
    AND s.metric_type = 'cpu'
WHERE e.is_valid = TRUE
    AND e.started_at IS NOT NULL
GROUP BY 
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', e.started_at),
    DATE(e.started_at),
    EXTRACT(HOUR FROM e.started_at),
    e.execution_type,
    e.duration_category,
    e.project_id;

-- Mart: User behavior for product insights
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.mart_user_behavior AS
SELECT 
    -- Dimensions
    DATE(u.created_at) AS interaction_date,
    u.user_id,
    u.session_id,
    u.interaction_type,
    u.project_id,
    
    -- Behavioral metrics
    COUNT(*) AS total_interactions,
    COUNT(DISTINCT u.interaction_type) AS unique_interaction_types,
    MAX(u.session_sequence) AS session_length,
    
    -- Time metrics
    MIN(u.created_at) AS first_interaction_time,
    MAX(u.created_at) AS last_interaction_time,
    EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (MAX(u.created_at) - MIN(u.created_at))) AS session_duration_seconds,
    
    -- Project engagement
    COUNT(DISTINCT u.project_id) AS projects_touched,
    
    -- Execution correlation
    COUNT(DISTINCT e.execution_id) AS executions_triggered,
    
    -- Derived metrics
    CASE 
        WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT u.project_id) > 1 THEN 'multi_project_user'
        WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT u.interaction_type) > 3 THEN 'explorer_user'
        ELSE 'basic_user'
    END AS user_segment
    
FROM staging.stg_user_interactions u
LEFT JOIN staging.stg_execution_logs e 
    ON u.project_id = e.project_id
    AND ABS(EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (u.created_at - e.started_at))) < 300 -- within 5 minutes
WHERE u.is_valid = TRUE
GROUP BY 
    DATE(u.created_at),
    u.user_id,
    u.session_id,
    u.interaction_type,
    u.project_id;

-- ============================================
-- 4. INDEXES for performance
-- ============================================

-- Raw layer indexes
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_projects_created_at ON raw.projects(created_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_execution_logs_project_id ON raw.execution_logs(project_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_execution_logs_started_at ON raw.execution_logs(started_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_user_interactions_created_at ON raw.user_interactions(created_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_raw_system_metrics_collected_at ON raw.system_metrics(collected_at);

-- Staging layer indexes
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_stg_projects_project_id ON staging.stg_projects(project_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_stg_execution_logs_composite ON staging.stg_execution_logs(project_id, started_at);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_stg_execution_logs_status ON staging.stg_execution_logs(status);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_stg_user_interactions_session_id ON staging.stg_user_interactions(session_id);

-- Marts layer indexes
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_mart_project_metrics_date ON marts.mart_project_metrics(metric_date);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_mart_execution_analytics_hour ON marts.mart_execution_analytics(execution_hour);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_mart_user_behavior_user_id ON marts.mart_user_behavior(user_id);

-- ============================================
-- 5. VIEWS for common queries
-- ============================================

-- View: Daily project health dashboard
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW marts.vw_daily_project_health AS
SELECT 
    metric_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT project_id) AS active_projects,
    SUM(total_executions) AS total_daily_executions,
    SUM(successful_executions) AS successful_executions,
    SUM(failed_executions) AS failed_executions,
    ROUND(SUM(successful_executions) * 100.0 / NULLIF(SUM(total_executions), 0), 2) AS success_rate_pct,
    SUM(total_tokens_used) AS daily_tokens_used,
    SUM(total_estimated_cost) AS daily_cost_usd,
    AVG(avg_duration_ms) AS avg_execution_duration_ms
FROM marts.mart_project_metrics
GROUP BY metric_date
ORDER BY metric_date DESC;

-- View: Hourly system load vs executions
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW marts.vw_hourly_system_load AS
SELECT 
    execution_hour,
    SUM(total_executions) AS executions_count,
    SUM(total_cost_usd) AS hourly_cost,
    AVG(avg_system_load) AS avg_cpu_load,
    SUM(total_executions) / 60.0 AS executions_per_minute
FROM marts.mart_execution_analytics
GROUP BY execution_hour
ORDER BY execution_hour DESC;

-- View: User retention metrics
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW marts.vw_user_retention AS
SELECT 
    user_id,
    MIN(interaction_date) AS first_seen_date,
    MAX(interaction_date) AS last_seen_date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT interaction_date) AS active_days,
    COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS total_sessions,
    COUNT(*) AS total_interactions,
    user_segment,
    COUNT(DISTINCT project_id) AS projects_created
FROM marts.mart_user_behavior
GROUP BY user_id, user_segment
ORDER BY active_days DESC;

-- ============================================
-- 6. dbt models directory structure
-- ============================================
/*

├── models/
│   ├── staging/
│   │   ├── schema.yml
│   │   ├── stg_projects.sql
│   │   ├── stg_execution_logs.sql
│   │   ├── stg_user_interactions.sql
│   │   └── stg_system_metrics.sql
│   ├── marts/
│   │   ├── schema.yml

│   │   ├── mart_execution_analytics.sql

│       └── macros/

## 1. Configuração de Segurança (src/config/security-config.js)

```javascript
// src/config/security-config.js
const crypto = require('crypto');

class SecurityConfig {
    constructor() {
        this.jwtConfig = {
            accessTokenExpiry: '15m', // SLA: Tokens com expiração curta
            refreshTokenExpiry: '7d',
            algorithm: 'HS256',
            issuer: 'diyapp-v10',
            audience: 'diyapp-services'
        };

        this.rateLimiting = {
            authAttempts: 5, // SLA: Bloqueio após N tentativas
            windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
            maxRequestsPerWindow: 100
        };

        this.inputValidation = {
            maxInputLength: 10000,
            allowedHtmlTags: [], // Nenhuma tag HTML permitida por padrão
            disallowedPatterns: [
                /<script\b[^<]*(?:(?!<\/script>)<[^<]*)*<\/script>/gi,
                /javascript:/gi,
                /on\w+\s*=/gi,
                /eval\(/gi,
                /union\s+select/gi,
                /drop\s+table/gi,
                /insert\s+into/gi,
                /delete\s+from/gi,
                /--/g,
                /\/\*/g,
                /\*\//g
            ]
        };

        this.filePermissions = {
            defaultFileMode: 0o644, // rw-r--r--
            sensitiveFileMode: 0o600, // rw-------
            directoryMode: 0o755, // rwxr-xr-x
            disallowedPaths: [
                /\.\.\//, // Path traversal
                /\/etc\//,
                /\/proc\//,
                /\/sys\//,
                /\/root\//,
                /\/var\/log\//
            ]
        };

        this.cryptoConfig = {
            algorithm: 'aes-256-gcm',
            keyLength: 32,
            ivLength: 16,
            saltRounds: 12
        };

        // Gerar secret seguro se não existir
        this.jwtSecret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || this.generateSecureSecret();
        this.encryptionKey = process.env.ENCRYPTION_KEY || this.generateSecureSecret(32);
    }

    generateSecureSecret(length = 64) {
        return crypto.randomBytes(length).toString('hex');
    }

    validateConfig() {
        const errors = [];
        
        if (!this.jwtSecret || this.jwtSecret.length < 32) {
            errors.push('JWT_SECRET deve ter pelo menos 32 caracteres');
        }
        
        if (!process.env.NODE_ENV) {
            errors.push('NODE_ENV deve ser definido');
        }
        
        return errors;
    }
}

module.exports = new SecurityConfig();
```

## 2. Implementação JWT entre Serviços (src/auth/jwt.js)

```javascript
// src/auth/jwt.js
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security-config');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class JWTService {
    constructor() {
        this.secret = securityConfig.jwtSecret;
        this.refreshTokens = new Map(); // Em produção, usar Redis
        this.revokedTokens = new Set(); // Tokens revogados
    }

    // SLA: Tokens com expiração curta (access: 15min, refresh: 7d)
    generateTokens(userId, roles = [], serviceId = null) {
        const accessToken = jwt.sign(
            {
                sub: userId,
                roles: roles,
                service: serviceId,
                type: 'access'
            },
            this.secret,
            {
                expiresIn: securityConfig.jwtConfig.accessTokenExpiry,
                issuer: securityConfig.jwtConfig.issuer,
                audience: securityConfig.jwtConfig.audience
            }
        );

        const refreshToken = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
        const refreshTokenHash = this.hashToken(refreshToken);
        
        // Armazenar refresh token (em produção, usar DB com TTL)
        this.refreshTokens.set(refreshTokenHash, {
            userId,
            roles,
            serviceId,
            expiresAt: Date.now() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) // 7 dias
        });

        return { accessToken, refreshToken };
    }

    verifyToken(token, options = {}) {
        try {
            // Verificar se token foi revogado
            if (this.revokedTokens.has(this.hashToken(token))) {
                throw new Error('Token revogado');
            }

            const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.secret, {
                issuer: securityConfig.jwtConfig.issuer,
                audience: securityConfig.jwtConfig.audience,
                ...options
            });

            return decoded;
        } catch (error) {
            logger.security(`Falha na verificação do token: ${error.message}`);
            throw error;
        }
    }

    refreshAccessToken(refreshToken) {
        const refreshTokenHash = this.hashToken(refreshToken);
        const tokenData = this.refreshTokens.get(refreshTokenHash);

        if (!tokenData) {
            throw new Error('Refresh token inválido');
        }

        if (Date.now() > tokenData.expiresAt) {
            this.refreshTokens.delete(refreshTokenHash);
            throw new Error('Refresh token expirado');
        }

        // Gerar novo access token
        return this.generateTokens(
            tokenData.userId,
            tokenData.roles,
            tokenData.serviceId
        ).accessToken;
    }

    // SLA: Invalidação de tokens no logout
    revokeToken(token) {
        const tokenHash = this.hashToken(token);
        this.revokedTokens.add(tokenHash);
        
        // Limpar tokens revogados antigos periodicamente
        setTimeout(() => {
            this.revokedTokens.delete(tokenHash);
        }, 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // Limpar após 24h
    }

    revokeAllUserTokens(userId) {
        // Em produção, implementar busca e revogação de todos os tokens do usuário
        for (const [hash, data] of this.refreshTokens.entries()) {
            if (data.userId === userId) {
                this.refreshTokens.delete(hash);
            }
        }
    }

    hashToken(token) {
        return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(token).digest('hex');
    }

    // Validação de escopo para comunicação entre serviços
    validateServiceToken(token, requiredService) {
        const decoded = this.verifyToken(token);
        
        if (decoded.type !== 'service') {
            throw new Error('Token não é de serviço');
        }
        
        if (requiredService && decoded.service !== requiredService) {
            throw new Error('Serviço não autorizado');
        }
        
        return decoded;
    }
}

module.exports = new JWTService();
```

## 3. Middleware de Autenticação e Autorização (src/auth/middleware.js)

```javascript
// src/auth/middleware.js
const jwtService = require('./jwt');
const securityConfig = require('../config/security-config');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class AuthMiddleware {
    constructor() {
        this.rateLimitStore = new Map(); // Em produção, usar Redis
        this.failedAttempts = new Map();
    }

    // Middleware de autenticação JWT
    authenticate(req, res, next) {
        try {
            const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
            
            if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
                return res.status(401).json({ 
                    error: 'Token de autenticação necessário',
                    code: 'AUTH_TOKEN_REQUIRED'
                });
            }

            const token = authHeader.substring(7);
            const decoded = jwtService.verifyToken(token);

            // Adicionar informações do usuário à requisição
            req.user = {
                id: decoded.sub,
                roles: decoded.roles || [],
                service: decoded.service
            };

            // Log de auditoria para operações privilegiadas
            if (decoded.roles && decoded.roles.some(r => r.includes('admin'))) {
                logger.audit(`Acesso admin: ${decoded.sub} - ${req.method} ${req.path}`);
            }

            next();
        } catch (error) {
            logger.security(`Autenticação falhou: ${error.message}`);
            
            return res.status(401).json({ 
                error: 'Token inválido ou expirado',
                code: 'INVALID_TOKEN'
            });
        }
    }

    // Middleware de autorização baseada em papéis
    authorize(requiredRoles = [], requireAll = false) {
        return (req, res, next) => {
            if (!req.user) {
                return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Não autenticado' });
            }

            const userRoles = req.user.roles || [];
            
            let authorized = false;
            
            if (requireAll) {
                // Requer todos os papéis
                authorized = requiredRoles.every(role => userRoles.includes(role));
            } else {
                // Requer pelo menos um dos papéis
                authorized = requiredRoles.some(role => userRoles.includes(role));
            }

            if (!authorized && requiredRoles.length > 0) {
                logger.security(`Tentativa de acesso não autorizado: ${req.user.id} - ${req.path}`);
                return res.status(403).json({ 
                    error: 'Acesso não autorizado',
                    code: 'INSUFFICIENT_PERMISSIONS'
                });
            }

            next();
        };
    }

    // SLA: Rate limiting em endpoints de autenticação
    rateLimitAuth(req, res, next) {
        const ip = req.ip;
        const now = Date.now();
        const windowMs = securityConfig.rateLimiting.windowMs;
        
        // Limpar tentativas antigas
        const attempts = this.failedAttempts.get(ip) || [];
        const recentAttempts = attempts.filter(time => now - time < windowMs);
        
        // SLA: Bloqueio temporário após N tentativas falhas
        if (recentAttempts.length >= securityConfig.rateLimiting.authAttempts) {
            logger.security(`Bloqueio por rate limiting: ${ip}`);
            return res.status(429).json({
                error: 'Muitas tentativas. Tente novamente mais tarde.',
                retryAfter: Math.ceil((windowMs - (now - recentAttempts[0])) / 1000)
            });
        }

        // Middleware para contar tentativas falhas
        const originalSend = res.send;
        res.send = function(data) {
            if (res.statusCode === 401) {
                recentAttempts.push(now);
                failedAttempts.set(ip, recentAttempts);
            }
            originalSend.call(this, data);
        };

        next();
    }

    // Middleware para validação de serviço a serviço
    serviceAuth(requiredService) {
        return (req, res, next) => {
            try {
                const serviceToken = req.headers['x-service-token'];
                
                if (!serviceToken) {
                    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token de serviço necessário' });
                }

                const decoded = jwtService.validateServiceToken(serviceToken, requiredService);
                req.service = decoded.service;
                
                next();
            } catch (error) {
                logger.security(`Autenticação de serviço falhou: ${error.message}`);
                return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Serviço não autorizado' });
            }
        };
    }

    // Prevenção de IDOR (Insecure Direct Object Reference)
    validateResourceOwnership(resourceOwnerIdField = 'userId') {
        return (req, res, next) => {
            if (!req.user) {
                return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Não autenticado' });
            }

            // Verificar se o usuário está acessando seu próprio recurso
            const resourceOwnerId = req.params[resourceOwnerIdField] || req.body[resourceOwnerIdField];
            
            if (resourceOwnerId && resourceOwnerId !== req.user.id) {
                // Verificar se é admin (pode acessar recursos de outros)
                if (!req.user.roles.includes('admin')) {
                    logger.security(`Tentativa de IDOR: ${req.user.id} tentou acessar recurso de ${resourceOwnerId}`);
                    return res.status(403).json({ 
                        error: 'Acesso ao recurso não autorizado',
                        code: 'RESOURCE_OWNERSHIP_VIOLATION'
                    });
                }
            }

            next();
        };
    }
}

module.exports = new AuthMiddleware();
```

## 4. Sistema de Permissões (src/auth/permissions.js)

```javascript
// src/auth/permissions.js
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class PermissionSystem {
    constructor() {
        // Princípio do menor privilégio
        this.rolePermissions = {
            // SLA: Principle of least privilege em todos os papéis
            'user': [
                'read:own_profile',
                'update:own_profile',
                'create:own_content',
                'read:public_content'
            ],
            'editor': [
                'read:own_profile',
                'update:own_profile',
                'create:own_content',
                'read:public_content',
                'update:own_content',
                'delete:own_content',
                'read:all_public'
            ],
            'admin': [
                'read:*',
                'update:*',
                'delete:*',
                'create:*',
                'manage:users',
                'manage:system'
            ],
            'service': [
                'service:internal',
                'read:system_metrics',
                'write:logs'
            ]
        };

        this.resourcePatterns = new Map();
    }

    // Verificação de permissão por recurso (não apenas por rota)
    checkPermission(userRoles, action, resource) {
        // Coletar todas as permissões do usuário baseado em seus papéis
        const userPermissions = new Set();
        
        userRoles.forEach(role => {
            const permissions = this.rolePermissions[role] || [];
            permissions.forEach(perm => userPermissions.add(perm));
        });

        // Verificar permissão específica
        const requiredPermission = `${action}:${resource}`;
        
        // Verificar permissão curinga
        const wildcardPermission = `${action}:*`;
        
        return userPermissions.has(requiredPermission) || 
               userPermissions.has(wildcardPermission) ||
               this.checkPatternPermission(userPermissions, action, resource);
    }

    // Suporte a padrões de recursos
    checkPatternPermission(userPermissions, action, resource) {
        for (const [pattern, permission] of this.resourcePatterns) {
            if (resource.match(pattern)) {
                const requiredPermission = `${action}:${permission}`;
                if (userPermissions.has(requiredPermission)) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    // Registrar padrão de recurso
    registerResourcePattern(pattern, permissionType) {
        this.resourcePatterns.set(new RegExp(pattern), permissionType);
    }

    // Middleware de autorização granular
    authorizeAction(action, resource) {
        return (req, res, next) => {
            if (!req.user || !req.user.roles) {
                return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Não autenticado' });
            }

            const hasPermission = this.checkPermission(
                req.user.roles,
                action,
                resource
            );

            if (!hasPermission) {
                logger.audit(`Tentativa de ação não autorizada: ${req.user.id} - ${action}:${resource}`);
                return res.status(403).json({ 
                    error: 'Permissão insuficiente para esta ação',
                    code: 'ACTION_NOT_PERMITTED'
                });
            }

            next();
        };
    }

    // Validação de escopo para tokens OAuth-like
    validateScope(requiredScopes) {
        return (req, res, next) => {
            const tokenScopes = req.user?.scopes || [];
            
            const hasAllScopes = requiredScopes.every(scope => 
                tokenScopes.includes(scope)
            );
            
            if (!hasAllScopes) {
                return res.status(403).json({
                    error: 'Escopo de token insuficiente',
                    missingScopes: requiredScopes.filter(s => !tokenScopes.includes(s))
                });
            }
            
            next();
        };
    }
}

module.exports = new PermissionSystem();
```

// src/security/input-sanitizer.js
const securityConfig = require('../config/security-config');

class InputSanitizer {
    constructor() {
        this.sanitizers = new Map();
        this.registerDefaultSanitizers();
    }

    registerDefaultSanitizers() {
        // Sanitizador para strings (prevenção XSS, SQLi)
        this.registerSanitizer('string', (value) => {
            if (typeof value !== 'string') {
                return String(value);
            }

            let sanitized = value;
            
            // Remover padrões maliciosos

### `tests/e2e/cypress/support/commands.js`

```javascript
// Comandos customizados para testes E2E
Cypress.Commands.add('login', (email, password) => {
  cy.session([email, password], () => {
    cy.visit('/login')
    cy.get('[data-cy="email-input"]').type(email)
    cy.get('[data-cy="password-input"]').type(password)
    cy.get('[data-cy="login-button"]').click()
    cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard')
    cy.get('[data-cy="user-avatar"]').should('be.visible')
  })
})

Cypress.Commands.add('createAgent', (agentType, config = {}) => {
  cy.get('[data-cy="new-agent-button"]').click()
  cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-type-${agentType}"]`).click()
  
  if (config.name) {
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-name-input"]').clear().type(config.name)
  }
  
  if (config.instructions) {
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-instructions-textarea"]').type(config.instructions)
  }
  
  cy.get('[data-cy="create-agent-button"]').click()
  cy.get('[data-cy="agent-status-active"]', { timeout: 10000 }).should('be.visible')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('sendMessageToAgent', (agentName, message) => {
  cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-card-${agentName}"]`).click()
  cy.get('[data-cy="agent-chat-input"]').type(message)
  cy.get('[data-cy="send-message-button"]').click()
  cy.get('[data-cy="agent-response"]', { timeout: 15000 }).should('be.visible')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('enableHiveMode', () => {
  cy.get('[data-cy="hive-mode-toggle"]').click()
  cy.get('[data-cy="hive-mode-active"]', { timeout: 5000 }).should('be.visible')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('assertLLMResponseQuality', (responseElement, criteria) => {
  cy.get(responseElement).then($el => {
    const response = $el.text()
    
    // Critérios de qualidade para respostas de LLM
    if (criteria.maxLength) {
      expect(response.length).to.be.lessThan(criteria.maxLength)
    }
    
    if (criteria.minLength) {
      expect(response.length).to.be.greaterThan(criteria.minLength)
    }
    
    if (criteria.contains) {
      criteria.contains.forEach(term => {
        expect(response.toLowerCase()).to.include(term.toLowerCase())
      })
    }
    
    if (criteria.notContains) {
      criteria.notContains.forEach(term => {
        expect(response.toLowerCase()).not.to.include(term.toLowerCase())
      })
    }
    
    // Verificar formatação (se aplicável)
    if (criteria.format === 'markdown') {
      expect(response).to.match(/(#{1,6}|- \[(x| )\]|\*\*.*\*\*|`.*`)/)
    }
  })
})
```

## 2. Testes E2E Principais

### `tests/e2e/cypress/e2e/dashboard-workflow.cy.js`

```javascript
describe('Dashboard Workflow - Fluxos Críticos', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser').email, Cypress.env('testUser').password)
  })

  it('CT-001: Deve carregar o dashboard com métricas em tempo real', () => {
    cy.visit('/dashboard')
    
    // Verificar componentes essenciais
    cy.get('[data-cy="agents-active-count"]').should('be.visible')
    cy.get('[data-cy="tasks-completed-today"]').should('be.visible')
    cy.get('[data-cy="system-health-status"]').should('have.text', 'Healthy')
    cy.get('[data-cy="recent-activity-feed"]').should('be.visible')
    
    // Verificar atualização em tempo real (WebSocket)
    cy.wait(3000)
    cy.get('[data-cy="metrics-updated-at"]').then($el => {
      const timestamp = new Date($el.text()).getTime()
      const now = Date.now()
      expect(now - timestamp).to.be.lessThan(10000) // Atualizado nos últimos 10s
    })
  })

  it('CT-002: Deve criar e gerenciar agentes', () => {
    const agentName = `QA-Agent-${Date.now()}`
    
    // Criar agente
    cy.createAgent('developer', {
      name: agentName,
      instructions: 'Você é um agente QA especializado em testes automatizados.'
    })
    
    // Verificar criação
    cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-card-${agentName}"]`).should('be.visible')
    cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-status-${agentName}"]`).should('have.text', 'Active')
    
    // Testar comunicação básica
    cy.sendMessageToAgent(agentName, 'Qual é sua especialidade?')
    cy.assertLLMResponseQuality('[data-cy="agent-response"]:last', {
      contains: ['QA', 'testes', 'automatizados'],
      maxLength: 500
    })
    
    // Pausar agente
    cy.get(`[data-cy="pause-agent-${agentName}"]`).click()
    cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-status-${agentName}"]`).should('have.text', 'Paused')
    
    // Reativar agente
    cy.get(`[data-cy="resume-agent-${agentName}"]`).click()
    cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-status-${agentName}"]`).should('have.text', 'Active')
    
    // Excluir agente
    cy.get(`[data-cy="delete-agent-${agentName}"]`).click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="confirm-delete-button"]').click()
    cy.get(`[data-cy="agent-card-${agentName}"]`).should('not.exist')
  })

  it('CT-003: Deve executar tarefas em lote via Hive Mode', () => {
    // Habilitar Hive Mode
    cy.enableHiveMode()
    
    // Criar múltiplos agentes
    const agents = ['Agent-1', 'Agent-2', 'Agent-3']
    agents.forEach(agentName => {
      cy.createAgent('task', { name: agentName })
    })
    
    // Criar tarefa em lote
    cy.get('[data-cy="create-batch-task"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="batch-task-description"]').type('Executar análise de código em paralelo')
    cy.get('[data-cy="assign-to-all-agents"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="start-batch-execution"]').click()
    
    // Monitorar execução paralela
    cy.get('[data-cy="batch-progress"]', { timeout: 30000 }).should('have.text', '100%')
    
    // Verificar resultados
    agents.forEach(agentName => {
      cy.get(`[data-cy="task-result-${agentName}"]`).should('be.visible')
      cy.get(`[data-cy="task-status-${agentName}"]`).should('have.text', 'Completed')
    })
    
    // Verificar que não há race conditions
    cy.get('[data-cy="concurrent-execution-errors"]').should('have.text', '0')
  })

  it('CT-004: Deve lidar com falhas graciosamente', () => {
    // Testar cenários de erro
    cy.intercept('POST', `${Cypress.env('apiUrl')}/agents`, {
      statusCode: 500,
      body: { error: 'Internal server error' }
    }).as('createAgentError')
    
    cy.get('[data-cy="new-agent-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-type-developer"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="create-agent-button"]').click()
    
    // Verificar tratamento de erro
    cy.get('[data-cy="error-message"]').should('be.visible')
    cy.get('[data-cy="error-message"]').should('contain', 'Erro ao criar agente')
    cy.get('[data-cy="retry-button"]').should('be.visible')
    
    // Restaurar intercept
    cy.intercept('POST', `${Cypress.env('apiUrl')}/agents`, {
      statusCode: 201,
      body: { success: true }
    })
    
    // Testar retry
    cy.get('[data-cy="retry-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-status-active"]', { timeout: 10000 }).should('be.visible')
  })
})
```

### `tests/e2e/cypress/e2e/agent-communication.cy.js`

```javascript
describe('Comunicação entre Agentes - Testes E2E', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser').email, Cypress.env('testUser').password)
  })

  it('CT-005: Agentes devem colaborar em tarefas complexas', () => {
    // Criar equipe de agentes especializados
    cy.createAgent('planner', { name: 'Planner-Agent' })
    cy.createAgent('developer', { name: 'Developer-Agent' })
    cy.createAgent('qa', { name: 'QA-Agent' })
    
    // Iniciar workflow colaborativo
    cy.get('[data-cy="start-collaboration-workflow"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="workflow-description"]').type('Desenvolver e testar feature de login')
    
    // Atribuir papéis
    cy.get('[data-cy="assign-role-Planner-Agent"]').select('Architect')
    cy.get('[data-cy="assign-role-Developer-Agent"]').select('Implementer')
    cy.get('[data-cy="assign-role-QA-Agent"]').select('Tester')
    
    cy.get('[data-cy="start-collaboration"]').click()
    
    // Monitorar comunicação entre agentes
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-message-Planner-Agent"]', { timeout: 15000 })
      .should('contain', 'plano')
      .and('be.visible')
    
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-message-Developer-Agent"]', { timeout: 15000 })
      .should('contain', 'implementar')
      .and('be.visible')
    
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-message-QA-Agent"]', { timeout: 15000 })
      .should('contain', 'testar')
      .and('be.visible')
    
    // Verificar resultado final
    cy.get('[data-cy="collaboration-result"]', { timeout: 30000 })
      .should('contain', 'Workflow completo')
      .and('contain', 'Planner-Agent')
      .and('contain', 'Developer-Agent')
      .and('contain', 'QA-Agent')
  })

  it('CT-006: Deve detectar e resolver conflitos entre agentes', () => {
    // Criar agentes com instruções conflitantes
    cy.createAgent('developer', {
      name: 'Agent-Node',
      instructions: 'Sempre use Node.js e JavaScript para tudo'
    })
    
    cy.createAgent('developer', {
      name: 'Agent-Python',
      instructions: 'Sempre use Python para tudo, é superior'
    })
    
    // Iniciar discussão técnica
    cy.get('[data-cy="start-technical-debate"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="debate-topic"]').type('Melhor linguagem para APIs REST')
    cy.get('[data-cy="start-debate"]').click()
    
    // Verificar conflito detectado
    cy.get('[data-cy="conflict-detected"]', { timeout: 10000 }).should('be.visible')
    
    // Verificar resolução automática
    cy.get('[data-cy="conflict-resolution"]', { timeout: 20000 })
      .should('contain', 'consenso')
      .or('contain', 'mediado')
    
    // Verificar que ambos agentes continuam funcionais
    cy.sendMessageToAgent('Agent-Node', 'Você ainda prefere Node.js?')
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-response"]:last')
      .should('contain', 'Node.js')
    
    cy.sendMessageToAgent('Agent-Python', 'E você, ainda prefere Python?')
    cy.get('[data-cy="agent-response"]:last')
      .should('contain', 'Python')
  })

  it('CT-007: Comunicação via Event Bus deve ser confiável', () => {
    // Habilitar logs do Event Bus
    cy.get('[data-cy="enable-event-bus-logs"]').click()
    
    // Criar publisher e subscriber
    cy.createAgent('publisher', { name: 'Event-Publisher' })
    cy.createAgent('subscriber', { name: 'Event-Subscriber' })
    
    // Configurar subscription
    cy.get('[data-cy="configure-subscription-Event-Subscriber"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="subscribe-to-topic"]').type('system.alerts')
    cy.get('[data-cy="save-subscription"]').click()
    
    // Publicar evento
    cy.get('[data-cy="publish-event-Event-Publisher"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-cy="event-topic"]').type('system.alerts')
    cy.get('[data-cy="event-payload"]').type('{"level": "warning", "message": "Test alert"}')
    cy.get('[data-cy="publish-button"]').click()
    
    // Verificar recebimento
    cy.get('[data-cy="event-received-Event-Subscriber"]', { timeout: 10000 })
      .should('contain', 'system.alerts')
      .and('contain', 'Test alert')
    
    // Verificar não-perda de eventos
    cy.get('[data-cy="events-published-count"]').then($pub => {
      cy.get('[data-cy="events-received-count"]').then($rec => {
        const published = parseInt($pub.text())
        const received = parseInt($rec.text())
        expect(received).to.be.at.least(published * 0.95) // Máximo 5% de perda
      })
    })
  })
})
```

## 1. Documentação da API (OpenAPI 3.0)

### `docs/api/openapi.yaml`
```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: DIYAPP Evolution V10 API
  description: |
    API do sistema autônomo DIYAPP Evolution V10.
    Sistema de gerenciamento de projetos com IA, operação 100% autônoma e arquitetura baseada em agentes.
    
    **Autenticação**: Bearer Token ou API Key
    **Base URL**: https://api.diyapp-v10.example.com/v1
    **Contato**: squad-autonoma@diyapp.example.com
    
    📋 **Status da API**: 
    - ✅ Produção estável
    - 🔄 Modo Hive ativo para refatoração paralela
    - 📊 Monitoramento 24/7 com SRE autônomo
  version: "10.0.0"
  termsOfService: https://diyapp.example.com/terms
  contact:
    name: Squad Autônoma V10
    email: tech-support@diyapp.example.com
  license:
    name: Proprietary
    url: https://diyapp.example.com/license

servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp-v10.example.com/v1
    description: Produção (100% autônomo)
  - url: https://staging-api.diyapp-v10.example.com/v1
    description: Staging (Modo Hive ativo)
  - url: http://localhost:3000/v1
    description: Desenvolvimento local

tags:
  - name: Projects
    description: Gerenciamento de projetos e tarefas
    externalDocs:
      description: Guia completo de projetos
      url: https://docs.diyapp.example.com/projects
  - name: Agents
    description: Gerenciamento de agentes autônomos
    externalDocs:
      description: Arquitetura de agentes
      url: https://docs.diyapp.example.com/agents
  - name: Hive Mode
    description: Operações do Modo Hive para refatoração paralela
  - name: Monitoring
    description: Endpoints de monitoramento e saúde do sistema
  - name: Authentication
    description: Autenticação e autorização

paths:
  /health:
    get:
      tags:
        - Monitoring
      summary: Verifica saúde do sistema
      description: |
        Retorna status detalhado de todos os componentes do sistema autônomo.
        Inclui status do Modo Hive, agentes ativos, banco de dados e serviços externos.
        
        **Uso por**: SRE autônomo, sistemas de monitoramento
        **Frequência**: A cada 30 segundos
      operationId: getHealthStatus
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Sistema saudável
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/HealthStatus'
              examples:
                healthy:
                  summary: Sistema operacional normal
                  value:
                    status: "healthy"
                    timestamp: "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
                    version: "10.0.0"
                    components:
                      database: 
                        status: "connected"
                        latency_ms: 12
                      redis:
                        status: "connected"
                        memory_used_mb: 245
                      hive_mode:
                        status: "active"
                        parallel_refactors: 3
                        stability_score: 0.98
                      agents:
                        total: 15
                        active: 15
                        by_type:
                          tech_lead: 1
                          dev_backend: 2
                          dev_frontend: 2
                          sre: 1
                          product_owner: 1
                          qa_engineer: 1
                          ux_designer: 1
                          tech_writer: 1
                          innovation: 1
                          compliance: 1
                          data_scientist: 1
                          security_engineer: 1
                          ai_ops: 1
        '503':
          description: Sistema com problemas
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
              examples:
                degraded:
                  summary: Sistema degradado
                  value:
                    error: "system_degraded"
                    message: "Hive mode experiencing instability"
                    details:
                      failing_component: "hive_coordination"
                      suggested_action: "Check hive coordinator logs"
                    timestamp: "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
      security:
        - ApiKeyAuth: []
        - BearerAuth: []

  /projects:
    get:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Lista projetos
      description: |
        Retorna lista paginada de projetos gerenciados pelo sistema.
        Inclui filtros por status, prioridade e agentes responsáveis.
        
        **Permissões necessárias**: `projects:read`
        **Rate Limit**: 100 requests/minuto
      operationId: listProjects
      parameters:
        - name: status
          in: query
          description: Filtro por status do projeto
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, completed, archived, blocked]
          example: active
        - name: limit
          in: query
          description: Número máximo de resultados (padrão: 20, máximo: 100)
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            maximum: 100
          example: 20
        - name: offset
          in: query
          description: Offset para paginação
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 0
          example: 0
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de projetos retornada com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectList'
        '401':
          description: Não autenticado
        '403':
          description: Permissões insuficientes
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
    
    post:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Cria novo projeto
      description: |
        Cria um novo projeto no sistema autônomo.
        O sistema automaticamente atribui agentes baseado no tipo de projeto.
        
        ⚠️ **Modo Hive**: Em refatorações paralelas, projetos podem ser realocados dinamicamente.
      operationId: createProject
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectCreate'
            examples:
              software_project:
                summary: Projeto de desenvolvimento de software
                value:
                  name: "E-commerce Platform V2"
                  description: "Refatoração completa da plataforma com microserviços"
                  type: "software_development"
                  priority: "high"
                  estimated_sprints: 8
                  requirements:
                    - "Migração para arquitetura de microserviços"
                    - "Implementação de cache distribuído"
                    - "Automação de deploys com CI/CD"
                  constraints:
                    max_budget: 50000
                    deadline: "2024-06-30"
                    compliance_requirements: ["GDPR", "PCI-DSS"]
      responses:
        '201':
          description: Projeto criado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
          headers:
            Location:
              description: URL do projeto criado
              schema:
                type: string
              example: /v1/projects/proj_abc123
        '400':
          description: Dados inválidos
        '409':
          description: Projeto com nome similar já existe
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
        - ApiKeyAuth: []

  /projects/{projectId}:
    get:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Obtém detalhes do projeto
      description: |
        Retorna detalhes completos de um projeto específico.
        Inclui status atual, agentes atribuídos, métricas e histórico do Modo Hive.
      operationId: getProject
      parameters:
        - name: projectId
          in: path
          required: true
          description: ID único do projeto
          schema:
            type: string
            pattern: '^proj_[a-zA-Z0-9]{24}$'
          example: "proj_abc123def456"
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Detalhes do projeto
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectDetail'
        '404':
          description: Projeto não encontrado
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []

    patch:
      tags:
        - Projects
      summary: Atualiza projeto
      description: |
        Atualiza parcialmente um projeto.
        Atualizações podem disparar reavaliação do Modo Hive para realocação de recursos.
        
        ⚠️ **Alterações críticas**: Mudanças de prioridade ou deadline podem acionar replanejamento automático.
      operationId: updateProject
      parameters:
        - name: projectId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectUpdate'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Projeto atualizado
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        '400':
          description: Dados inválidos
        '404':
          description: Projeto não encontrado
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []

  /hive/operations:
    get:
      tags:
        - Hive Mode
      summary: Lista operações do Modo Hive
      description: |
        Retorna operações ativas e recentes do Modo Hive.
        Inclui refatorações paralelas em andamento e histórico de realocações.
        
        **Acesso restrito**: Apenas agentes com permissão `hive:monitor`
      operationId: listHiveOperations
      parameters:
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, completed, failed, scheduled]
        - name: since
          in: query
          description: Filtra operações desde esta data (ISO 8601)
          schema:
            type: string
            format: date-time
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de operações
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/HiveOperationList'
        '403':
          description: Acesso negado ao Modo Hive
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
        - ApiKeyAuth: []

  /agents/{agentId}/status:
    get:
      tags:
        - Agents
      summary: Status do agente
      description: |
        Retorna status detalhado de um agente específico.
        Inclui carga de trabalho, saúde e métricas de performance.
        
        **Monitoramento**: Atualizado a cada 10 segundos pelo sistema autônomo.
      operationId: getAgentStatus
      parameters:
        - name: agentId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
            pattern: '^agent_[a-zA-Z0-9]{16}$'
          example: "agent_techlead_001"
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Status do agente
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentStatus'
        '404':
          description: Agente não encontrado
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []

  /monitoring/metrics:
    get:
      tags:
        - Monitoring
      summary: Métricas do sistema
      description: |
        Retorna métricas em tempo real do sistema autônomo.
        Formato compatível com Prometheus.
        
        **Uso primário**: Dashboard do SRE autônomo
      operationId: getSystemMetrics
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Métricas no formato Prometheus
          content:
            text/plain:
              schema:
                type: string
              example: |
                # HELP diyapp_system_stability_score Score de estabilidade do sistema (0-1)
                # TYPE diyapp_system_stability_score gauge
                diyapp_system_stability_score 0.98
                
                # HELP diyapp_hive_parallel_refactors Refatorações paralelas ativas
                # TYPE diyapp_hive_parallel_refactors gauge
                diyapp_hive_parallel_refactors 3
                
                # HELP diyapp_agents_active_total Agentes ativos
                # TYPE diyapp_agents_active_total gauge
                diyapp_agents_active_total 15
      security:
        - ApiKeyAuth: []

components:
  securitySchemes:
    BearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
      bearerFormat: JWT
      description: |
        Token JWT obtido via OAuth2.
        Escopos necessários variam por endpoint.
    ApiKeyAuth:
      type: apiKey
      in: header
      name: X-API-Key
      description: |
        API Key para integrações automáticas.
        Usado pelo SRE autônomo e sistemas de monitoramento.

  schemas:
    HealthStatus:
      type: object
      required:
        - status
        - timestamp
        - version
      properties:
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [healthy, degraded, unhealthy]
          description: Status geral do sistema
        timestamp:
          type: string
          format: date-time
          description: Horário da verificação
        version:
          type: string
          description: Versão da API
        components:
          type: object
          description: Status de componentes individuais
          properties:
            database:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/ComponentStatus'
            redis:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/ComponentStatus'
            hive_mode:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/HiveComponentStatus'
            agents:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentsStatus'

    ComponentStatus:
      type: object
      properties:
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [connected, disconnected, degraded]
        latency_ms:
          type: number
          description: Latência em milissegundos (se aplicável)
        last_check:
          type: string
          format: date-time

    HiveComponentStatus:
      allOf:
        - $ref: '#/components/schemas/ComponentStatus'
        - type: object
          properties:
            parallel_refactors:
              type: integer
              description: Número de refatorações paralelas ativas
            stability_score:
              type: number
              minimum: 0
              maximum: 1
              description: Score de estabilidade do Modo Hive
            coordination_mode:
              type: string
              enum: [centralized, decentralized, hybrid]
              description: Modo de coordenação atual

    AgentsStatus:
      type: object
      properties:
        total:
          type: integer
          description: Número total de agentes configurados
        active:
          type: integer
          description: Agentes atualmente ativos
        by_type:
          type: object
          additionalProperties:
            type: integer
          description: Contagem de agentes por tipo

    Project:
      type: object
      required:
        - id
        - name
        - status
        - created_at
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
          pattern: '^proj_[a-zA-Z0-9]{24}$'
          description: ID único do projeto
        name:
          type: string
          minLength: 3
          maxLength: 200
          description: Nome do projeto
        description:
          type: string
          maxLength: 1000
        status:
          type: string
          enum: [draft, planning, active, review, completed, archived, blocked]
        priority:
          type: string
          enum: [critical, high, medium, low]
          default: medium
        created_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        updated_at:
          type: string
          format: date-time
        assigned_agents:
          type: array
          items:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/AgentReference'

    ProjectCreate:
      type: object
      required:
        - name
        - type
      properties:
        name:
          type: string
          minLength: 3
          maxLength: 200
        description:
          type: string
          maxLength: 1000
        type:
          type: string
          enum: [software_development, infrastructure, data_analysis, research, maintenance]
        priority:
          type: string
          enum: [critical, high, medium, low]
          default: medium
        requirements:
          type: array
          items:
            type: string
          maxItems: 50
        constraints:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/ProjectConstraints'

    ProjectDetail:
      allOf:
        - $ref: '#/components/schemas/Project'
        - type: object

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Integração Low-Code e RAG

## Análise de Oportunidade

**SINAL IDENTIFICADO**: Crescimento acelerado de plataformas low-code (AppSmith, Retool, Budibase) como ferramentas padrão para dashboards internos e aplicações empresariais. Usuários finais demandam maior velocidade de desenvolvimento sem sacrificar customização.

**HIPÓTESE**: Acreditamos que **desenvolvedores de produto interno** têm o problema de **precisar criar interfaces administrativas e dashboards rapidamente** e que **exportar componentes DIYAPP como templates de AppSmith** vai resultar em **redução de 70% no tempo de desenvolvimento de dashboards internos**.

## Proposta de Implementação

Vou criar um sistema de exportação para AppSmith com RAG para contexto dos agentes:

```html
